// PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined
this.PageLoaded = function(location) {
        let vm = this.vm ?? {};
        vm.thinClient = thinClient.vm;
        // let httpClient = this.httpClient;

        clearInterval(thinClient.notificationIntervalId);

        if (location == '/') document.location = '#!/shipping'
        else if (location == '/shipping') shipping();
        else if (location == '/history') history();

        function shipping () {
            vm.shipping = {
                panelMessage: '',
                loadValue: '[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]',
                notificationInterval: 1800000, //30 minutes
                // notificationInterval: 1200000, //20 minutes
                // notificationInterval: 5000, //5 seconds
                videoModal: {
                    selector: '#VideoModalId',
                    zoom: {
                        in: zoomIn,
                        out: zoomOut,
                    },
                    close: videoModalClose,
                    stream: {
                        selector: '#CameraStreamId',
                        start: videoStreamStart,
                        stop: videoStreamStop,
                        captureImage: captureImage
                    }
                },
                imageFile: {
                    selector: '#CarrierLabelImageId',
                    upload: uploadCarrierLabelFile
                },
                menu: {
                    guide: {
                        inputFile: {
                            selector: '#inputFileDownload',
                        }
                    }
                },
                load: loadShip,
                customerChange: customerChange,
                getNotification: getNotification,
                selectDownloadFile: selectDownloadFile
            }
            vm.shipping.videoModal.id = vm.shipping.videoModal.selector.substring(1);
            vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id = vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.selector.substring(1);
            vm.shipping.imageFile.id = vm.shipping.imageFile.selector.substring(1);
            vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.id = vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selector.substring(1);

            $(document).on('change', vm.shipping.imageFile.selector, uploadCarrierLabelFile);
            $(document).on('change', vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selector, inputFileDownloadChange);

            vm.shipping.slic = vm.UserInformation.SiteId ? vm.profile.Name.substring(0,5) : vm.profile.Name == thinClient.adminProfileName ? "XXXXX" : null;
            vm.shipping.customers = getShipperCustomers(vm.profile.Shippers);
            var enabledCustomers = vm.shipping.customers.filter(function(c) { return c.disabled != true; });
            vm.shipping.customer = enabledCustomers.length == 1 ? vm.shipping.customers[1] : vm.shipping.customers[0];
            vm.shipping.activePanel = vm.shipping.slic == undefined || vm.clientContext.Machine.Name == undefined ? 0 : 1;

            debugger;

            vm.fieldOptions = {
                Consignee: {
                    hideSaveAddress: true,
                    hideAddressSearch: true,
                    hideValidateAddress: true
                },
                ReturnAddress: {
                    hideSaveAddress: true,
                    hideAddressSearch: true,
                    hideValidateAddress: true
                }
            };
            vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference18.IsDisabled = true;
            vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference20.DefaultValue = vm.shipping.slic;
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20 = vm.shipping.slic;

            activate();

            function activate() {
                if (!vm.profile.FieldOptions?.Reference?.IsHidden)
                    'form[name="referenceForm"] .panel > div'.unwrap();

                'name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"] div[active="activeSubtabIndex"]'.remove();
                'name-address[address-property-name="ReturnAddress"] div[ng-hide="poBox.isHidden()"'.remove();
                'name-address[address-property-name="ReturnAddress"] div[active="activeSubtabIndex"]'.remove();
                'name-address[address-property-name="ReturnAddress"] div[ng-hide="residential.isHidden()"'.remove();


                vm.shipping.getNotification();
                thinClient.notificationIntervalId = setInterval(function() {
                    vm.shipping.getNotification();
                }, vm.shipping.notificationInterval);

                if (vm.shipping.customer.disabled)
                    vm.shipping.customer.selector.focus();
                else
                    vm.shipping.loadValue.focus();
            }

            function getNotification() {
                var data = { CompanyId: vm.clientContext.Company.Id }
                thinClient.httpClient('GetClientNotifications', data).then(function (ret) {
                    if (!vm.shipping.setNotification(ret.Notifications)) {
                        if (vm.clientContext.Site.Name == undefined)
                            vm.notification = null;
                        else {
                            var data = { CompanyId: vm.clientContext.Company.Id, SiteId: vm.clientContext.Site.Id };
                            thinClient.httpClient('GetClientNotifications', data).then(function (ret) {
                                if (!vm.shipping.setNotification(ret.Notifications))
                                    vm.notification = null;

                                vm.thinClient.loadData.show();
                            })
                        }
                    }
                    vm.thinClient.loadData.show();
                })

                this.setNotification = function(notifications) {
                    var notification = notifications.at(-1);
                    if (notification == undefined) return false;

                    this.notification = {
                        Title: thinClient.htmlText(notification.Title),
                        Message: thinClient.htmlText(notification.Message)
                    }
                    return true;
                }
            }

            function selectDownloadFile(event) {
                this.menu.guide.selectedDownloadFile = event.target.innerText;
                if (this.menu.guide.inputFile.selected) {
                    if (this.menu.guide.selectedDownloadFile.slice(-3) == this.menu.guide.inputFile.selected.name.slice(-3))
                        updateFile();
                } else {
                    var payload = { Action: 'downloadFile', Data: this.menu.guide.selectedDownloadFile };
                    var data = { UserContext: undefined, Data: JSON.stringify(payload) };
                    thinClient.httpClient('UserMethod', data).then(function (ret) {
                        if (ret.ErrorCode === 0) {
                            var data = JSON.parse(atob(ret.Data));

                            let linkData = `data:${data.fileType};base64,${data.encodedFile}`;
                            let downloadLink = document.createElement("a");
                            downloadLink.style.display = "none";
                            downloadLink.download = data.fileName;
                            downloadLink.href = linkData;
                            document.body.appendChild(downloadLink);
                            downloadLink.click();
                            document.body.removeChild(downloadLink);
                        }
                    });
                }

                function updateFile() {
                    var reader = new FileReader();
                    reader.onload = function () {
                        var request = {
                            Key: vm.shipping.menu.guide.selectedDownloadFile,
                            Value: JSON.stringify({
                                fileType: vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selected.type,
                                fileName: vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selected.name,
                                encodedFile: this.result.split(',')[1]
                            })
                        }
                        var payload = { Action: 'updateFile', Data: request };
                        var data = { UserContext: undefined, Data: JSON.stringify(payload) };
                        thinClient.httpClient('UserMethod', data).then(function (ret) {
                            if (ret.ErrorCode !== 0)
                                vm.notificationService.notifyDanger(ret.ErrorCode + " - " + ret.ErrorMessage);
                        }).catch(function (response) {
                            vm.notificationService.notifyDanger(vm.translations.Common.ErrorConnectingWCFService + ": " + response.status + " " + response.statusText);
                        })
                        vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selected = null;
                        $(vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selector).val(null);
                        vm.thinClient.loadData.show();

                    }
                    if (vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selected) reader.readAsDataURL(vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selected);
                }
            }

            function inputFileDownloadChange(event) {
                if (event.target.files == undefined) return;
                vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selected = event.target.files[0];
                vm.thinClient.loadData.show();
            }

            function getShipperCustomers(shippers) {
                var shipper = shippers.find(shipper => shipper.Symbol == vm.shipping.slic);
                if (shipper == undefined)
                     return [{ name: '--- No Shipper Configured ---', disabled: true }];

                var customData = shipper.CustomData.filter(c => c.Key.toUpperCase() == "CUSTOMER");
                var customers = customData.map(function(c) {
                    var customer = c.Value.toUpperCase();

                    if (customer == 'AMAZON')
                        return { name: "Amazon", value: customer, hasLoad: true, hasReturn: true, autoShip: true };
                    else if (customer == 'UPS')
                        return { name: "UPS", value: customer, hasCameraImage: true, hasFileImage: true, autoShip: false };
                    else if (customer == 'DEMO')
                        return { name: "Demo", value: customer, hasLoad: false, hasReturn: true, hasCameraImage: true, hasFileImage: false, autoShip: false };
                    else if (customer == 'FANATICS')
                        return { name: "Fanatics", value: customer, hasReturn: true, hasCameraImage: true, autoShip: false };
                    else
                        return { name: `--- ${customer} ---`, disabled: true };
                });

                customers.sort(function(a, b) {
                    if (a.disabled && !b.disabled) return 1;
                    if (!a.disabled && b.disabled) return -1;
                    return a.name.localeCompare(b.name);
                });
                return [{ name: '--- Select Customer Option ---', selector: 'select[ng-model="vm.shipping.customer"]', disabled: true }].concat(customers);
            }

            function customerChange() {
                vm.shipping.loadValue.focus();
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference19 = vm.shipping.customer.value;
            }


            function videoModalClose () {
                var $videoModal = $(vm.shipping.videoModal.selector);
                if ($videoModal.is(':visible'))
                    $videoModal.find('.close').click();
            }

            function uploadCarrierLabelFile () {
                var $carrierLabelImage = $(vm.shipping.imageFile.selector);
                var imageFile = $carrierLabelImage.prop('files')[0];
                if (imageFile == undefined) {
                    $carrierLabelImage.click();
                    return;
                }
                var reader = new FileReader();
                reader.readAsDataURL(imageFile);
                reader.onload = function () {
                    var dataURL = this.result;
                    getMegapixelsFromFileReader(dataURL).then(function(megapixels) {
                        console.log(`The image is ${megapixels.toFixed(2)} megapixels.`);
                    });

                    vm.loadValue = 'Label Upload';
                    vm.labelImage = dataURL.replace(/^data:.+;base64,/, '');
                    vm.load();
                    $carrierLabelImage.val(null);
                }
            }

            function captureImage () {
                // vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id = vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.selector
                var cameraStream = document.getElementById(vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id);
                var track = cameraStream.srcObject.getVideoTracks()[0];
                var imageCapture = new ImageCapture(track);

                imageCapture.grabFrame().then(function(imageBitmap) {
                    const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
                    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');

                    // Set canvas dimensions to match the imageBitmap
                    canvas.width = imageBitmap.width;
                    canvas.height = imageBitmap.height;

                    // Draw the imageBitmap onto the canvas
                    ctx.drawImage(imageBitmap, 0, 0);

                    // Get the image data as a Base64 data URL
                    // You can specify format and quality (e.g., 'image/jpeg', 0.8)
                    const base64DataUrl = canvas.toDataURL('image/png', 1.0);
                    // var newTab = window.open('about:blank','image from canvas');
                    // newTab.document.write("<img src='" + base64DataUrl + "' alt='from canvas'/>");

                    vm.loadValue = 'Label Capture';
                    vm.labelImage = base64DataUrl.replace(/^data:.+;base64,/, '');
                    // vm.videoModal.stopVideoStream();
                    vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.stop();
                    vm.load();
                })


                // imageCapture.takePhoto().then(function(blob) {
                //     var reader = new FileReader();
                //     reader.readAsDataURL(blob);
                //     reader.onloadend = function () {
                //         var dataURL = reader.result;
                //         getMegapixelsFromFileReader(dataURL).then(function(megapixels) {
                //             console.log(`The image is ${megapixels.toFixed(2)} megapixels.`);
                //         });

                //         vm.loadValue = 'Label Capture';
                //         vm.labelImage = dataURL.replace(/^data:.+;base64,/, '');
                //         vm.videoModal.stopVideoStream();

                //         vm.load();
                //     }
                // })
            }

            function getMegapixelsFromFileReader(fileData) {
                return new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
                    var img = new Image();
                    img.src = fileData;
                    img.onload = function () {
                        var width = this.naturalWidth;
                        var height = this.naturalHeight;
                        console.log(`Image dimensions: ${width}x${height}`);
                        var megapixels = (width * height) / 1000000;
                        resolve(megapixels);
                    }
                })
            }

            function videoStreamStop(isCanceled) {
                vm.labelImage = isCanceled ? null : vm.labelImage;

                var cameraStream = document.getElementById(vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id);
                if (cameraStream.srcObject) {
                    var tracks = cameraStream.srcObject.getTracks();
                    tracks.forEach(track => track.stop()); // Stop each track in the stream
                    cameraStream.srcObject = null;
                }
            }


            function videoStreamStart () {
                if (navigator.mediaDevices && navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia) {
                    // Request access to the video stream
                    var constraints = {
                        audio: false,
                        video: {
                            zoom: true,
                            facingMode: 'environment',
                            // aspectRatio: { ideal: 9/16 }
                        }
                    };
                    //HD
                    // constraints.video.width = { ideal: 1920 };
                    // constraints.video.height = { ideal: 1080 };

                    //QHD
                    constraints.video.width = { ideal: 2560 };
                    constraints.video.height = { ideal: 1440 };

                    //4K UHD
                    // constraints.video.width = { ideal: 3840 };
                    // constraints.video.height = { ideal: 2160 }

                    navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia(constraints).then(function(stream) {
                        // Assign the stream to the video element's source object
                        var cameraStream = document.getElementById(vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id);
                        cameraStream.srcObject = stream;

                        var [track] = stream.getVideoTracks();
                        var capabilities = track.getCapabilities();

                        vm.videoModal.zoom ??= {
                            min: capabilities.zoom.min,
                            max: capabilities.zoom.max,
                            current: track.getSettings().zoom
                        }
                        var zoomLevel = localStorage.getItem('zoomLevel') ?? getZoomLevel(track.getSettings().zoom);

                        track.applyConstraints({ advanced: [{ zoom: zoomLevel }] });
                        vm.videoModal.track = track;
                        // if (capabilities.zoom) {
                        //     track.applyConstraints({ advanced: [{ zoom: capabilities.zoom.max }] });
                        // }
                    }).catch(function(error) {
                        console.error("Error accessing the camera: ", error);
                    });
                } else {
                    // Fallback for older browsers
                    console.error("Your browser does not support the getUserMedia API.");
                }

                function getZoomLevel(currentZoom) {
                    localStorage.setItem('zoomLevel', currentZoom);
                    return currentZoom;
                }
            }

            function zoomOut() {
                // localStorage.setItem("settings", JSON.stringify(userSettings));
                var zoomLevel = Number(localStorage.getItem('zoomLevel'));
                if (zoomLevel > vm.videoModal.zoom.min) {
                    zoomLevel -= 100;
                    localStorage.setItem('zoomLevel', zoomLevel);
                    vm.videoModal.track.applyConstraints({ advanced: [{ zoom: zoomLevel }] });
                }
            }

            function zoomIn() {
                var zoomLevel = Number(localStorage.getItem('zoomLevel'));
                if (zoomLevel < vm.videoModal.zoom.max) {
                    zoomLevel += 100;
                    localStorage.setItem('zoomLevel', zoomLevel);
                    vm.videoModal.track.applyConstraints({ advanced: [{ zoom: zoomLevel }] });
                }
            }

            function loadShip(shipmentRequest) {
                debugger;
                vm.load();
                if (vm.shipping.customer.autoShip) {
                    vm.intervalId = setInterval(function(shipmentRequest) {
                        console.log(shipmentRequest != vm.currentShipment)
                        if (shipmentRequest != vm.currentShipment) {
                            clearInterval(vm.intervalId);
                            // if(!(vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage ?? '').includes('Invalid Service Option'))
                                vm.ship();
                        }
                    }, 20, shipmentRequest)
                }
            }
        }

        function history() {
            vm.history = {
                searchButton: 'button:contains("Search")',
                reportSelector: '#reports'
            };

            $(document).on('click', vm.history.searchButton, selectReportChange);
            $(document).on('change', vm.history.reportSelector, selectReportChange);

            activate();

            function activate() {
                if (vm.profile.Name != vm.thinClient.adminProfileName) {
                    vm.hideButtonExport = true;

                    let reports = [ 'Default', 'Detailed Report', 'Void Report', 'Summary Report' ];
                    vm.reports = vm.reports.filter(function(report) {
                        report.TemplateHtml = report.TemplateHtml.replace(/<span.*glyphicon-search.*<\/span>/g, '');
                        return reports.includes(report.Name);
                    });
                }
            }

            function selectReportChange(event) {
                if (vm.report?.Name == 'Summary Report') {
                    vm.hideButtonExport = true;
                    vm.history.carrierAcceptTableContainer = {
                        'height': $('.panel-body').height() + 'px',
                        'overflow-y': 'auto'
                    };

                    let payload = {
                        Action: 'summaryReport',
                        Data: {
                            startDate: vm.dtstart.toLocaleDateString('en-CA'),
                            endDate: vm.dtend.toLocaleDateString('en-CA'),
                            sites: getSites()
                        }
                    };
                    let data = { UserContext: undefined, Data: JSON.stringify(payload) };
                    thinClient.httpClient('UserMethod', data).then(function (ret) {
                        debugger;
                        vm.history.carrierAcceptReport = JSON.parse(atob(ret.Data));
                        vm.thinClient.loadData.show();
                    });
                } else {
                    vm.hideButtonExport = false;
                }

                function getSites() {
                    let sites = vm.UserInformation.SiteId ? vm.sites.filter(function(site) { return site.Id == vm.UserInformation.SiteId;}) : vm.sites;
                    return sites.map(function(site) { return { name: site.Name }; });
                }
            }
        }
    } // returns undefined

    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) { 
        
          $(function ()
  {

    {

$('[nameaddress="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee"]').find($('input[ng-model="nameaddress.Account"]').attr('ng-required', true).css('border-color', '#a94442'));
      }

    });
  });

// this.Shipping() // returns undefined
    this.Shipping = function () {
        $('body').on('change', client.shipping.fileInputPaperless, this.vm, paperlessChange);
  
         function paperlessChange(e) {
             var file = e.target.files[0]
             if (file === undefined) {
                e.data.paperless = null;
             }
             else {
                 var reader = new FileReader();
                 reader.readAsDataURL(file);
                 reader.onloadend = function () {
                     e.data.paperless = { fileName: file.name, fileData: this.result.split(',')[1] }
                 }
             }                
         }       
     }

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        debugger;
        $(client.shipping.fileInputPaperless)?.val(null)?.change();

        $(function () {
            $('body').delegate('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Terms"]', 'change', function () {

                var chkBox = $('input[type=checkbox][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]');
                var chkVal = $(chkBox).prop('checked');


                if (($(this).val() === 'string:SHIPPER') && (chkVal === false))//Freight Collect -> uncheck 3rd party billing box
                {
                    $(chkBox).click();
                    //$('[nameaddress="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee"]').find($('input[ng-model="nameaddress.Account"]').attr('ng-required', true).css('border-color', '#a94442'));
                    $('[nameaddress="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee"]').find($('input[ng-model="nameaddress.Account"]').attr('ng-required', 'account.isRequired()').css('border', '1px solid #ccc'));
                }

                else if (($(this).val() === 'string:CONSIGNEE') && (chkVal === true))//Prepaid -> check 3rd party billing box
                {
                    $(chkBox).click();

// function NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        if (cbr.historyShipment != null) {
            var historyRequest = JSON.parse(cbr.historyShipment);
            this.vm.totalPackages = historyRequest.Packages.length;

            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults = historyRequest.PackageDefaults;
            shipmentRequest.Packages = historyRequest.Packages;
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Description = "PC Equipment";

            shipmentRequest.Packages.forEach(function (pkg) {
                pkg.ReturnDelivery = true;
                pkg.ReturnDeliveryMethod = 4;
                pkg.ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail = historyRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email;
                pkg.Description = "PC Equipment";
            });
            cbr.historyShipment = null;
        }
        cbr.bulk.create.itemReferences = [];
    }

// function BatchManager() // returns undefined
this.BatchManager = function () {
        clickUploadFile();

        function clickUploadFile() {
            $('body').delegate('button:contains("Upload File")', 'click', function () {
                if ($('#fileInputField').val() != '') {
                    showSpinner();
                    var interval = setInterval(function () {
                        var msg = $('div[role="alert"]:visible');
                        if (msg.length > 0) {
                            clearInterval(interval);
                            hideSpinner();
                        }
                    }, 50);
                }
            })
        }
    }

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
		//debugger;
		vmTemp = this.vm;
		
		console.log(vmTemp);

		shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].CommodityClass = "CLASS_65";
		//document.getElementById("autoship_checkbox").checked = false;
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20 = false;   // autoship checkbox

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service) {
			shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol = "x";
		}

		// clear Markup Percentage
		$("#custom_markup_id").val("");

		// set dialog values/events
		$('#newOrderNumber').val('');
		$('#newWeight').val('');
		$('#newWeight').keypress(function(e) {
			// enforce weight mask
			if (!String.fromCharCode(e.which).match(/[0-9.]+/g)) {
				return false;
			}
		})
		$('#newBoxType').change(function() {
			if ($(this).find('option:selected').val() !== '') {
				// show dimensions string if box was selected
				let length = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Length;
				let width = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Width;
				let height = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Height;
				let units = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Units === 0 ? "IN" : "CM";
				$('#newDimensions').val(length + "x" + width + "x" + height + " " + units);
				
				if (vmTemp.loadValue) {
					$('#newShipmentDialog button[ng-click="vm.load()"').prop('disabled', false);
				}
			}
			else {
				$('#newDimensions').val('');
			}
		});
		$('#newDimensions').val('');
		$('#newDimensions').keyup(function(e) {
			let loadButton = $('#newShipmentDialog button[ng-click="vm.load()"');
			if (this.value.trim() === '' && vmTemp.loadValue) {
				loadButton.prop('disabled', false);
			}
			else {
				// enforce dimensions mask if entered LxWxH (IN/CM optional)
				let regEx = /(\d+)x(\d+)x(\d+)( IN| CM)?/
				if (!regEx.test(this.value)) {
					loadButton.prop('disabled', true);
				}
				else if (vmTemp.loadValue) {
					loadButton.prop('disabled', false);
				}
			}
		});

		// show Load Shipment dialog and set focus
		if (!$('#newShipmentDialog').is(':visible')) {
			$('#newShipmentDialog').modal('show');
			$('#newShipmentDialog').on('shown.bs.modal', function() {
				$(this).find('[autofocus]').focus();
			});
		}
	};

// this.PreLoad(value, shipmentRequest, params) // returns undefined
this.PreLoad = function(value, shipmentRequest, params) {
		//debugger;
		if (shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].BoxType === undefined || shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].BoxType === null) {
			// if box is empty, add custom dimensions from dialog
			let dims = $('#newDimensions').val().trim().split(/x| /);
			if (dims !== null && dims.length >= 3) {
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('input[name="length"]').val(dims[0]).change();
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('input[name="width"]').val(dims[1]).change();
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('input[name="height"]').val(dims[2]).change();
				
				let index = 1;
				if (dims.length === 4) {
					dims[3] = dims[3].toUpperCase();
					index = (dims[3] === 'IN' ? 1 : 2);
				}
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('select[name="units"] option:eq(' + index + ')').prop('selected', true);
			}
		}

		let oChk = this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20;		// autoship
		if (oChk === true) {
			params.autoship = oChk;
		}

		$('#newShipmentDialog').modal('hide');
		showLoading(true);
	};

// this.PostLoad(value, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.PostLoad = function(value, shipmentRequest) {
		debugger;
		let errorMessage = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage;
		
		if (errorMessage === undefined) errorMessage = "";
		if (errorMessage === null) errorMessage = "";

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service !== undefined && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol === "x") {
			showLoading(false);
			alert("No service selected!");
		}
		
		if (errorMessage !== undefined && errorMessage === 'validate') {
			//$("#ctl00_cphContent_left_tabs_consignee_tab_consignee_na_ab_ctrl_na_ctrl_validate_addr_btn").click();
			showLoading(false);
			return;
		}

		if (errorMessage !== undefined && errorMessage.substring(0, 4) === "pop:") {
			showLoading(false);
			alert(errorMessage.substring(4));
			return;
		}

		if (errorMessage !== undefined && errorMessage !== '') {
			showLoading(false);
			alert(errorMessage);
			let errors = ["not found", "already shipped", "too many"];
			if (errors.some(errorText => errorMessage.includes(errorText))) {
				// open Load Shipment dialog
				this.vm.newShipment();
			}
			return;
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country === 'US') {
			this.vm.shipMode = 1;
		} else {
			this.vm.shipMode = 0;
		}

		$("#custom_markup_id").val(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3);

		//getWeight();

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 === 'autoship') {
			this.vm.checkShip();
			return;
		}

		// select all services before rate
		setTimeout(function() {
			// check Select All after delay to allow UI update
			vmTemp.isAllServicesSelected = true;
			vmTemp.selectAllServices();
			vmTemp.rate();
		}, 100);
		
	};

// init() // returns void
init: function () {          
            String.prototype.addButtonLabel = function(text) {
                var interval = setInterval(function(selector) { 
                    var $element = $(selector);
                    if ($element.length) {
                        clearInterval(interval);                        
                        $element.parent().removeClass('col-md-3');
                        $element.parent().addClass('col-md-4'); 
                        $element.wrap('<label class="ng-binding">').after(text);
                    } 
                }, 10, this);
            }
        },

// ShowPackVerifyDialog(CommodityContents, ShipperReference) // returns void
      ShowPackVerifyDialog: function (CommodityContents, ShipperReference)
      {
        /* Delete and re-create the individual container tables.
          <table class="table-custom" id="tablePackVerifyCutTicketScanResults">
            <tbody>
              <tr>
                <th>Order #</th>
                <th>Item #</th>
                <th>Qty</th>
                <th>Total</th>
                <th style="width: 32px;"></th>
              </tr>
              <tr class="empty-table">
                <td colspan="6" style="text-align: center;">No items placed in container.</td>
              </tr>
            </tbody>
          </table>
        */
        try
        {
          /* Get rid of any previous container tables, then create a new empty one. */
          /* This is more efficient than looking for possible existing table(s) and dealing with them. */
          $('div.table-box-contents').find('table').remove().promise().done(function (e)
          {
            var tableResults = $('<table />').addClass('table-custom').attr('id', 'tablePackVerifyCutTicketScanResults');

            $(tableResults).append($('<tr />')
              .append($('<th />').text('Order #'))
              .append($('<th />').text('Item #'))
              .append($('<th />').text('Qty'))
              .append($('<th />').text('Total'))
              .append($('<th />').css('width', '32px')));

            $(tableResults).append($('<tr />').addClass('empty-table')
              .append($('<td />')
                .attr('colspan', '6')
                .css('text-align', 'center')
                .text('No items placed in container.')));

            $('div.table-box-contents').append($(tableResults));

          });

          $('span.total-container-count').text('1');
          $('span.current-container-index').text('1');
          $('span.box-pkg-count').text('0');

          $('#divModalPackVerify').fadeIn(200).promise().done(function ()
          {
            // $('body').delegate('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].BoxType"]', 'change', function (e)
            // {
            //   $('#selectClonedBoxTypes').first().prop('selectedIndex', $(this).prop('selectedIndex'));
            //   $('#selectClonedBoxTypes').first().trigger('change').trigger('click');
            // });

            var i = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].BoxType"]').prop('selectedIndex');

            $('#selectClonedBoxTypes').prop('selectedIndex', i).trigger('change');
            $('span.order-number-list').text(ShipperReference);

            ShowOverlay();

            PackVerify.AddCommoditiesToTable(CommodityContents);

            $('#inputScanCutTicket').focus();

          });
        }
        catch (error)
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: GetCallingFunctionName(), Error: error, Data: CommodityContents });
          HideOverlay();
        }
      }

      },

// ConsolidatedOrders.InitElements() // returns void
      InitElements: function()
      {
        /* Create the Consolidate Orders button dynamically. */
        /* This is done on the post load for my customer as they want to have a primary order loaded first. */
        /* With each consolidated order being added, I am comparing the consignee to the primary order to confirm this order is going to the correct consignee. */
        $('div.top-tool-bar > div.pull-left').append($('<button />')
          .addClass('btn btn-xs btn-primary')
          .attr('id', 'buttonConsolidateOrders')
          .text('Consolidate Orders').fadeIn());

        /* Set up all delegates from within this block. */
        $('body').delegate('#buttonConsolidateOrders', 'click', function(e)
        {
          ConsolidatedOrders.ShowConsolidatedOrderDialog();
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonAddOrderNumbers', 'click', function(e)
        {
          ConsolidatedOrders.AddOrderNumbersToList();
        });

        /* Customer uses a scanner that appends the <enter> key after the scan.  This delegate fires when that happens. */
        $('body').delegate('#textOrderNumber', 'keyup', function(e)
        {
          var keycode = e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which;
          if ((keycode == 13) | (keycode == 9))
          {
            ConsolidatedOrders.AddOrderNumbersToList();
          }
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonSaveConsolidatedOrders', 'click', function(e)
        {
          ConsolidatedOrders.SaveConsolidatedOrderNumbers();
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonCloseConsolidatedOrdersWithoutSaving', 'click', function(e)
        {
          ConsolidatedOrders.CloseDialogWithoutSaving();
        });

      }

// Source: FalconNDX (FNDX)_Falcon_CBR_1794.cs
// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function(location) { 
        debugger;
        
        //Days List
        const days = ["Sunday","Monday","Tuesday","Wednesday","Thursday","Friday","Saturday"];
         
        // Current Date
        var dt = new Date();  
       //dt.setDate(dt.getDate()  +1);
        //alert(dt);
        
        //Finding Last Date of the Month
        var lastDate=new Date(dt.getFullYear(),dt.getMonth()+1 ,0);
        var onlyDate_lastDate= lastDate.getDate();
       
        
          
        //Months List  
        var month= dt.getMonth()+1;
        var nextmonth =dt.getMonth()+1;  //Get the current month
        
        
        //Year
        var currentYear = dt.getFullYear();
  
        
        
                
        var nextdate=dt.getDate()+1;    
        var newdate=dt.getDate()+2;
        
        
        
        /* Comparing current date(saturday/sunday) with lastdate of the month
        1. Current date and last date is saturday 
        2. Next to Current date and last date is saturday */
        
        /* Scenarios
        1. Current date - Saturday , Last date - Sunday 
            Next to current date should match with last date.
        2. Current date - Sunday , Last date - Sunday
            Current date should match with last date.
        3. Current date - Saturday , Last date - Saturday
        4. Current date - Sunday , Last date - Saturday
        
        
        
        */
        
       if(dt.getDate()== onlyDate_lastDate && days[dt.getDay()] == "Saturday")
       {
           
           if(month==12)
            {
                nextmonth=1; // Setting next month if current date is last date of the month eg: 31/07/2022 => 07 to 08
                newdate=2;
                currentYear=currentYear + 1;
            }else
            {
                 nextmonth=month +1; 
                  newdate=1;
                  currentYear=currentYear;
            }
            
            
           
           
       }
       
     
      else if(dt.getDate()== onlyDate_lastDate && days[dt.getDay()] == "Sunday")
       {
           
           if(month==12)
            {
                nextmonth=1; // Setting next month if current date is last date of the month eg: 31/07/2022 => 07 to 08
                newdate=1;
                currentYear=currentYear + 1;
            }else
            {
              
                 nextmonth=month +1; 
                  newdate=1;
                  currentYear=currentYear;
            }
            
            
           
           
       }
        else if(nextdate == onlyDate_lastDate )  
       {
            
             if(month==12)
            {
                nextmonth=1; // Setting next month if current date is last date of the month eg: 31/07/2022 => 07 to 08
                newdate=1;
                currentYear=currentYear + 1;
            }else
            {
                 nextmonth=month +1; 
                  newdate=1;
                  currentYear=currentYear;
            }
            
             
           
       }
       
     //Saturday to Monday 
       var monthIndex = nextmonth;
                if(monthIndex<10)
                monthIndex=('0'+monthIndex);
                
       var mondateIndex=newdate;
                if(mondateIndex<10)
                mondateIndex=('0'+mondateIndex);
                
       var lastdate=(currentYear+"-"+ monthIndex+"-"+mondateIndex);
        
     if(days[dt.getDay()] == "Saturday")
        {
            lastdate=(currentYear+"-"+ monthIndex+"-"+mondateIndex);
            $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(lastdate).change();
        }
         
         
      
      //Sunday to Monday   
         var sundateIndex=dt.getDate();
       
         if(dt.getDate()==onlyDate_lastDate)
            {
              
                 sundateIndex=newdate;   
                   
            }
            else
            {
               
                sundateIndex=dt.getDate()+1;
            }

        
          if(sundateIndex<10)
            sundateIndex=('0'+sundateIndex);
                     
           if(days[dt.getDay()] == "Sunday")
            {
                 lastdate=(currentYear+"-"+ monthIndex+"-"+sundateIndex);
                 $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(lastdate).change();
            }
           
    }

// function ClientBusinessRules() // returns object initialization and method assignments
function ClientBusinessRules() {
        var userContext;
    
    this.PageLoaded = function(location) {
        GetUserContext();
    };
    
   this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) { 
      var originCustomData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
       shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference   = GetKeyValue('Custom1', originCustomData);
       shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = GetKeyValue('Custom2', originCustomData);
      // shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = "Ground";
   };
   
   
   
    this.PreSearchHistory = function (searchCriteria) {
        searchCriteria.WhereClauses.push({ FieldName: 'MiscReference19', FieldValue: userContext.UserId, Operator: 5 });
    };
    
       this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
           var userId = userContext.UserId;
        for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++) {
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference19 = userId;
        }
       };
    
    /////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
   function GetKeyValue(key, arr) {
      for (var index in arr) {
          if (arr[index].Key.toLowerCase() === key.toLowerCase()) return arr[index].Value;
      }
      return '';
  }

function GetUserContext() {
    if (userContext === undefined) {
        userContext = ajaxGet('api/usercontext/GET');
    }
}
function ajaxGet(url) {
    var result;
    $.ajax({
        type: "GET",
        url: url,
        async: false,
        success: function(response) {
            result = response;
        }
    });
    return result;
}
// End ClientBusinessRules
}

// function GetUserContext() // returns userContext data via synchronous ajax
function GetUserContext() {
    if (userContext === undefined) {
        userContext = ajaxGet('api/usercontext/GET');
    }
}

// function ajaxGet(url) // returns ajax response object
function ajaxGet(url) {
    var result;
    $.ajax({
        type: "GET",
        url: url,
        async: false,
        success: function(response) {
            result = response;
        }
    });
    return result;
}

// Source: FortessaTS (FTS)_FortessaCBR_1897.cs
// this.Shipping() // returns undefined
this.Shipping = function () {
        this.vm.getWeight = customGetWeight;
        //shipperReferenceKeyUp();
        miscReference7KeyUp();
        replaceSelectBoxTypeWithInputText(this.vm.profile.BoxTypes);

        $('body').delegate(client.shipping.addPackageButton, 'keyup', function (e) {

            if (e.key === 'Tab' || e.key === "Enter") {
                //client.shipping.shipperReference.focus();
                client.shipping.miscRef7.focus();
            }
        })


        function shipperReferenceKeyUp() {
            $('body').delegate(client.shipping.shipperReference, 'keydown', function (e) {
                if (e.key === 'Tab' || e.key === "Enter") {
                    client.shipping.$inputBoxType.focus();
                }
            })
        }

        function miscReference7KeyUp() {
            $('body').delegate(client.shipping.miscRef7, 'keydown', function (e) {
                if (e.key === 'Tab' || e.key === "Enter") {
                    client.shipping.$inputBoxType.focus();
                }
            })
        }


        function customGetWeight() {
            if (this.profile.ScaleConfiguration) {
                var url = client.config.ClientSupportServiceUrl + '/api/Scale/Read'
                var ret = $.post({ url: url, data: this.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition, async: false }).responseJSON;
                if (ret != undefined) {
                    if (ret.ErrorCode == 0) {
                        this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight = {
                            "Amount": ret.Weight.toFixed(2),
                            "Units": ret.WeightUnit.toUpperCase()
                        };
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        function replaceSelectBoxTypeWithInputText(boxTypes) {
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                client.shipping.$selectBoxType = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].BoxType"]');
                if (client.shipping.$selectBoxType.length > 0) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    client.shipping.$inputBoxType = $('<input type="text" />').attr({ class: client.shipping.$selectBoxType.attr('class') });
                    client.shipping.$selectBoxType.hide();
                    client.shipping.$inputBoxType.insertAfter(client.shipping.$selectBoxType);

                    client.shipping.$inputBoxType.keyup(boxTypes, function (e) {
                        if (e.key === 'Tab' || e.key === "Enter") {
                            for (var boxType of e.data) {
                                if (boxType.Name == this.value) {
                                    this.value = '';
                                    client.shipping.$selectBoxType.val(boxType.Id).change();
                                    client.shipping.addPackageButton.focus();
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    });

                }
            }, 10);
        }




    }

// this.PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.PostLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        this.vm.getWeight();
		
        //scroll selected service into view
        scrollIntoView($('[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]'), shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol);
	
		//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 29, Year: 2024 }
        //this.vm.startshipdate.value = new Date(shipDate.Year, shipDate.Month, shipDate.Day);
        //shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
		
        //this.vm.overrideOptimization = pastDueDate(shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference6)
        pastDueDate(shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference6);
		
		//checkAndSetShipDate(this.vm);
		checkAndSetShipDateTest(this.vm);
		
        this.vm.arriveByDate = client.shipping.arriveByDate;
        client.shipping.$inputBoxType.focus();

        function pastDueDate(miscReference6) {
            //if (miscReference6 && miscReference6.trim().length != 0 && miscReference6 != '*1900-01-01T00:00:00*') {

            if (miscReference6 && miscReference6.trim().length != 0) {

                miscReference6 = miscReference6.replaceAll('*', '');
                client.shipping.arriveByDate = miscReference6.split("T")[0];

                var dateRequired = Date.parse(miscReference6);
                if (dateRequired <= Date.now() && miscReference6 != "1900-01-01T00:00:00") {
                    $('h1').removeClass('text-success').addClass('text-danger');
                    return true;
                }
                else {
                    $('h1').removeClass('text-danger').addClass('text-success');
                }
            };
            return false;
        }

        //scroll into view stuff
        function isIE() {
            return /*@cc_on!@*/false || !!document.documentMode;
        }

        function scrollIntoView(element, value) {
            if (!isIE()) {
                var interval = setInterval(function () {
                    if (element.val() == value) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        var optionTop = element.find('[value="' + value + '"]').offset().top;
                        var selectTop = element.offset().top;
                        element.scrollTop(element.scrollTop() + (optionTop - selectTop));
                    }
                }, 50);

            }

        }

		function checkAndSetShipDate(viewModel) {
            var hardCutoffTime = 6;
            var currentDateTime = new Date();//can simulate it being other dates and times by changing this value
            console.log("Current datetime returned: " + currentDateTime);
            var hours = currentDateTime.getHours();
            var dayOfWeek = currentDateTime.getDay();

            console.log("Hours: " + hours);
            console.log("Day: " + dayOfWeek);

            

            var dateInterval = setInterval(function () {
                var $shipDt = $('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]');

                if ($shipDt.length) {
                    clearInterval(dateInterval);
                    
                    if (dayOfWeek == 6) {
                        //day is saturday, add 2 days and return new date
                        var newDate = addDays(2);
						//var dateFinal = newDate.getFullYear()+'/'+(newDate.getMonth()+1)+'/'+newDate.getDate();
                        console.log("New Date: " + dateFinal);
						//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 29, Year: 2024 }
						viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(newDate.Year, newDate.Month, newDate.Day);
						shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
						//$('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(dateFinal).change();
                        //viewModel.startshipdate.value = newDate;
						//shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
                        //return;
                    }

                    if (hours >= hardCutoffTime) {
                        //cutoff time reached, change date as follows
                        if (dayOfWeek == 5) {
                            //add 3 days making Monday the ship date
                            var newDate = addDays(3);
							var dateFinal = newDate.getFullYear()+'/'+(newDate.getMonth()+1)+'/'+newDate.getDate();
                            console.log("New Date: " + dateFinal);
							viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(newDate.Year, newDate.Month, newDate.Day);
							shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
							//$('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(dateFinal).change();
                            //viewModel.startshipdate.value = newDate;
							//shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
                            //return;
                        }

                        else {
                            //add 1 day to the date making tomorrow the ship date
                            var newDate = addDays(1);
							var dateFinal = newDate.getFullYear()+'/'+(newDate.getMonth()+1)+'/'+newDate.getDate();
                            console.log("New Date: " + dateFinal);
							viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(newDate.Year, newDate.Month, newDate.Day);
							shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
							//$('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(dateFinal).change();
                            //viewModel.startshipdate.value = newDate;
							//shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
                            //return;
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
            

            

        }

        function addDays(days) {
            var date = new Date();
            date.setDate(date.getDate() + days);
			
			console
            return date;
        }
		
		function checkAndSetShipDateTest(viewModel)
		{
			debugger;
			var hardCutoffTime = 16;
			var currentDateTime = new Date();
			var hours = currentDateTime.getHours();
            var dayOfWeek = currentDateTime.getDay();
			
			if (dayOfWeek == 6) {
				var finalDate = addDays(2);
				console.log("New date" + finalDate);
				var month = finalDate.getMonth() + 1;
				var day = finalDate.getDate();
				var year = finalDate.getFullYear();
				console.log("Month " + month + " Day " + day + " Year " + year);
				//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 30, Year: 2024 }
				var shipDate = {Month: month, Day: day, Year: year};
				viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(shipDate.Year, shipDate.Month, shipDate.Day);
				shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
			}
			
			if (hours >= hardCutoffTime) {
				if (dayOfWeek == 5) {
					var finalDate = addDays(3);
					console.log("New date" + finalDate);
					var month = finalDate.getMonth() + 1;
					var day = finalDate.getDate();
					var year = finalDate.getFullYear();
					console.log("Month " + month + " Day " + day + " Year " + year);
					//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 30, Year: 2024 }
					var shipDate = {Month: month, Day: day, Year: year};
					viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(shipDate.Year, shipDate.Month, shipDate.Day);
					shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
				}
				
				else{
					var finalDate = addDays(1);
					console.log("New date" + finalDate);
					var month = finalDate.getMonth() + 1;
					var day = finalDate.getDate();
					var year = finalDate.getFullYear();
					console.log("Month " + month + " Day " + day + " Year " + year);
					//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 30, Year: 2024 }
					var shipDate = {Month: month, Day: day, Year: year};
					viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(shipDate.Year, shipDate.Month, shipDate.Day);
					shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
				}
				
			}
			
		}

    }

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {

        this.vm.overrideOptimization = false;
        this.vm.arriveByDate = '';
        $('h1').removeClass('text-danger').removeClass('text-success');
		
        client.shipping.loadValue.focus();
        client.shipping.maintabfocus('General');
        client.shipping.subtabfocus('Consignee', 'Account/Tax');

		

        //check and set the CPD checkbox here
        checkAndSetCPD(this.vm);


        //check for CPD flag here, set checked if true
        function checkAndSetCPD(viewModel) {
            //create interval here to watch for CPD checkbox
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                var $cpdCB = $('[ng-model="vm.cpdProcessFlow"]');

                if ($cpdCB.length) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    var cpdFlag = sessionStorage.getItem("cpdflag");
                    //status can be True, False or Null

                    if (cpdFlag == "true") {
                        viewModel.cpdProcessFlow = true;
                    }
                    else {
                        viewModel.cpdProcessFlow = false;
                    }


                }
            }, 10)

        }

		
    }

// this.AddPackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns undefined
this.AddPackage = function (shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
        this.vm.getWeight();

        if (this.vm.cpdProcessFlow) {
            //$(client.shipping.shipperReference).focus().select();
            $(client.shipping.miscRef7).focus().select();
        }
        else {
            client.shipping.$inputBoxType.focus();
        }
    }

        function  translateDates() {
            const monthMapping = {
                "January": "Janvier",
                "February": "Février",
                "March": "Mars",
                "April": "Avril",
                "May": "Mai",
                "June": "Juin",
                "July": "Juillet",
                "August": "Août",
                "September": "Septembre",
                "October": "Octobre",
                "November": "Novembre",
                "December": "Décembre"
                };
                
                const dayMapping = {
                  'Mon': 'Lun',
                  'Tue': 'Mar',
                  'Wed': 'Mer',
                  'Thu': 'Jeu',
                  'Fri': 'Ven',
                  'Sat': 'Sam',
                  'Sun': 'Dim'
                };


                const currentYear = new Date().getFullYear();
                $("small[aria-label]").each(function() {
                  var day = $(this).text().trim();
                  var translatedDay = dayMapping[day];
                  if (translatedDay) {
                    $(this).text(translatedDay);
                  }
                });
                
                $("strong").each(function() {
                  var dateText = $(this).text().trim();
                  var month = dateText.split(' ')[0];
                  var translatedMonth = monthMapping[month];
                  if (translatedMonth) {
                      var updatedText = dateText.replace(month, translatedMonth);
                      $(this).text(updatedText);
                  }
                });

                var buttonLeft = document.querySelector('.uib-left');
                var buttonRight = document.querySelector('.uib-right');
        
                if (buttonLeft) {
                    $(buttonLeft).off('click.custom').on('click.custom', function() {
                       return getCurrentMonthYear('previous');
                        // Your logic here
                    });
                }
                
                if (buttonRight) {
                    $(buttonRight).off('click.custom').on('click.custom', function() {
                       return getCurrentMonthYear('next');
                        // Your logic here
                    });
                }


            }

            function getCurrentMonthYear(action) {
                const frenchMonths = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                let monthYear = null;
               
                $('strong.ng-binding').each(function() {
                    let text = $(this).text();
                    
                    for (let i = 0; i < frenchMonths.length; i++) {
                        if (text.includes(frenchMonths[i])) {
                            if(action=='next') {
                                $(this).text(getNextMonthYearInFrench(text));
                            } else {
                                $(this).text(getPreviousMonthYearInFrench(text));
                            }
                            return false;  // Break out of the .each() loop
                        }
                    }
                });
                
                return monthYear;
            }


            function getNextMonthYearInFrench(dateStr) {
                var monthNamesFr = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                var splitDate = dateStr.split(' ');
                var month = splitDate[0];
                var year = splitDate[1];
            
                var currentMonthIndex = monthNamesFr.indexOf(month);
                
                // Check if the current month is December.
                if (currentMonthIndex === 11) {
                    // Increment the year and reset the month to January.
                    year++;
                    month = monthNamesFr[0];
                } else {
                    // Get the next month.
                    month = monthNamesFr[currentMonthIndex + 1];
                }
                
                return month + ' ' + year;
            }


            function getPreviousMonthYearInFrench(dateStr) {
                var monthNamesFr = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                var splitDate = dateStr.split(' ');
                var month = splitDate[0];
                var year = splitDate[1];
            
                var currentMonthIndex = monthNamesFr.indexOf(month);
                
                // Check if the current month is January.
                if (currentMonthIndex === 0) {
                    // Decrement the year and set the month to December.
                    year--;
                    month = monthNamesFr[11];
                } else {
                    // Get the previous month.
                    month = monthNamesFr[currentMonthIndex - 1];
                }
                
                return month + ' ' + year;
            }

            translateElements2: function(selector, translation, replacer) {
                $(selector).each(function() {
                    var text = $(this).val();
                    if (translation[text] !== undefined) {
                        replacer.call(this, text, translation[text]);
                    }
                });
            },
            translateElements: function(selector, translation, replacer) {
                $(selector).each(function() {
                    var text = $(this).text().trim();
                    if (translation[text] !== undefined) {
                        replacer.call(this, text, translation[text]);
                    }
                });
            },

            replaceText: function(oldText, newText) {
                this.innerHTML = this.innerHTML.replace(oldText, newText);
            },
            replaceText2: function(oldText, newText) {
                this.innerText = this.innerText.replace(oldText, newText);
            },

            replaceValue: function(oldText, newText) {
                $(this).val(newText);
            },

            replaceLabel: function(oldText, newText) {
                $(this).attr('label', newText);
            },
             replaceLabel2(selector, oldText, newText) {
                $(selector).each(function() {
                    if ($(this).attr('label') === oldText) {
                        $(this).attr('label', newText);
                    }
                });
            },

            handleSpecificCases: function() {
                $('h5:contains("No commodities added")').text('Aucune marchandise ajoutée');
                $('label.control-label.no-left-padding.ng-binding').each(function() {
                    if ($(this).attr('style') === "text-align: center" && $(this).html() === "&nbsp;of&nbsp;&nbsp;1") {
                        $(this).html('&nbsp;de&nbsp;&nbsp;1');
                    }
                });
            },
        };

// function translateDates() // returns undefined
        function  translateDates() {
            const monthMapping = {
                "January": "Janvier",
                "February": "Février",
                "March": "Mars",
                "April": "Avril",
                "May": "Mai",
                "June": "Juin",
                "July": "Juillet",
                "August": "Août",
                "September": "Septembre",
                "October": "Octobre",
                "November": "Novembre",
                "December": "Décembre"
                };
                
                const dayMapping = {
                  'Mon': 'Lun',
                  'Tue': 'Mar',
                  'Wed': 'Mer',
                  'Thu': 'Jeu',
                  'Fri': 'Ven',
                  'Sat': 'Sam',
                  'Sun': 'Dim'
                };


                const currentYear = new Date().getFullYear();
                $("small[aria-label]").each(function() {
                  var day = $(this).text().trim();
                  var translatedDay = dayMapping[day];
                  if (translatedDay) {
                    $(this).text(translatedDay);
                  }
                });
                
                $("strong").each(function() {
                  var dateText = $(this).text().trim();
                  var month = dateText.split(' ')[0];
                  var translatedMonth = monthMapping[month];
                  if (translatedMonth) {
                      var updatedText = dateText.replace(month, translatedMonth);
                      $(this).text(updatedText);
                  }
                });

                var buttonLeft = document.querySelector('.uib-left');
                var buttonRight = document.querySelector('.uib-right');
        
                if (buttonLeft) {
                    $(buttonLeft).off('click.custom').on('click.custom', function() {
                       return getCurrentMonthYear('previous');
                        // Your logic here
                    });
                }
                
                if (buttonRight) {
                    $(buttonRight).off('click.custom').on('click.custom', function() {
                       return getCurrentMonthYear('next');
                        // Your logic here
                    });
                }


            }

// function getCurrentMonthYear(action) // returns the monthYear value or null
            function getCurrentMonthYear(action) {
                const frenchMonths = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                let monthYear = null;
               
                $('strong.ng-binding').each(function() {
                    let text = $(this).text();
                    
                    for (let i = 0; i < frenchMonths.length; i++) {
                        if (text.includes(frenchMonths[i])) {
                            if(action=='next') {
                                $(this).text(getNextMonthYearInFrench(text));
                            } else {
                                $(this).text(getPreviousMonthYearInFrench(text));
                            }
                            return false;  // Break out of the .each() loop
                        }
                    }
                });
                
                return monthYear;
            }

// function getNextMonthYearInFrench(dateStr) // returns a French month-year string
            function getNextMonthYearInFrench(dateStr) {
                var monthNamesFr = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                var splitDate = dateStr.split(' ');
                var month = splitDate[0];
                var year = splitDate[1];
            
                var currentMonthIndex = monthNamesFr.indexOf(month);
                
                // Check if the current month is December.
                if (currentMonthIndex === 11) {
                    // Increment the year and reset the month to January.
                    year++;
                    month = monthNamesFr[0];
                } else {
                    // Get the next month.
                    month = monthNamesFr[currentMonthIndex + 1];
                }
                
                return month + ' ' + year;
            }

// function getPreviousMonthYearInFrench(dateStr) // returns a French month-year string
            function getPreviousMonthYearInFrench(dateStr) {
                var monthNamesFr = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                var splitDate = dateStr.split(' ');
                var month = splitDate[0];
                var year = splitDate[1];
            
                var currentMonthIndex = monthNamesFr.indexOf(month);
                
                // Check if the current month is January.
                if (currentMonthIndex === 0) {
                    // Decrement the year and set the month to December.
                    year--;
                    month = monthNamesFr[11];
                } else {
                    // Get the previous month.
                    month = monthNamesFr[currentMonthIndex - 1];
                }
                
                return month + ' ' + year;
            }

                this.translateMenuToFrench();
               
                  // Bind the translation function to the click event of the arrow elements in the date picker
            },

         function deliverDatePicker() {

            translateToFrench = {
                "Months": {
                  "January": "Janvier",
                  "February": "Février",
                  "March": "Mars",
                  "April": "Avril",
                  "May": "Mai",
                  "June": "Juin",
                  "July": "Juillet",
                  "August": "Août",

                  "Friday": "Vendredi",
                  "Saturday": "Samedi"
                }
              };

            var datePicker = $('div.uib-daypicker');
            var currentMonth = datePicker.find('th button strong');
            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(translateToFrench['Months'])) {
                if (currentMonth.text().indexOf(key) != -1) {
                    currentMonth.text(currentMonth.text().replace(key, value));
                }
            }



            datePicker.find('th small').each(function () {
                $(this).text(translateToFrench.Days[this.innerHTML]);
            })
        }

                var translationObj = this.createTranslationObjects();

                this.translateElements('select option', translationObj.optionLabelTranslation, this.replaceText);
                this.translateElements('label', translationObj.labeltTranslation, this.replaceText);
                this.translateElements('label', translationObj.labeltTranslation, this.replaceText2);
                this.translateElements('select option', translationObj.labeltTranslation, this.replaceLabel);
                this.translateElements('td.ng-binding', translationObj.tdTranslation, this.replaceText);
                this.translateElements('a', translationObj.aTranslation, this.replaceText);
                this.translateElements('select option', translationObj.packagingTypes, this.replaceLabel);
                this.handleSpecificCases();
            },

// function selectCanadaForAllCountrySelects() // returns undefined
    function selectCanadaForAllCountrySelects() {
        // Check if the flag is already true, which means we no longer need to change the selects
        if(canadaSelected || !isSelectedValueInShippersArray()) {
          return; // Exit the function if Canada has been selected in all dropdowns or if the site is not from Canada
        }
        
        // Get all select elements with the name 'Country'
        var selects = document.querySelectorAll('select[name="Country"]');
        var allSelected = true; // To keep track if all selects have been set to Canada
      
        // Iterate through the NodeList
        selects.forEach(function(select) {
          // Only set the value to 'string:CA' if it's not already set
          if (select.value !== 'string:CA') {
            select.value = 'string:CA';
            allSelected = false; // Not all selects have been set to Canada
      
            // Trigger change event for AngularJS
            if ('createEvent' in document) {
              var evt = document.createEvent('HTMLEvents');
              evt.initEvent('change', false, true);
              select.dispatchEvent(evt);
            } else {
              select.fireEvent('onchange');
            }
          }
        });
      
        // If all selects have been set to Canada, set the flag to true
        if (allSelected) {
          canadaSelected = true;
        }
      }

// function isSelectedValueInShippersArray() // returns boolean
      function isSelectedValueInShippersArray() {
        // Use a more specific selector that targets the ng-model
        var selectElement = document.querySelector('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"]');
        
        // Ensure the element exists
        if (!selectElement) {
          console.warn('Select element not found');
          return false;
        }
        
        // Get the index of the selected option
        var selectedIndex = selectElement.selectedIndex;
        
        // Ensure an option is selected
        if (selectedIndex < 0) {
          console.warn('No option is selected');
          return false;
        }
        
        // Get the selected option element
        var selectedOption = selectElement.options[selectedIndex];
        
        // Get the value of the selected option (and remove the "string:" prefix if present)
        var selectedValue = selectedOption.value.replace('string:', '');
        
        // Check if the selected value is in the array
        return StoreLocationsCanadaArray.includes(selectedValue);
      }

// function GetUserName() // returns the matched username string or null
function GetUserName() {
   var helloUser = $('a[title="Manage"]:contains("Hello")').text();
   return helloUser.match(/[a-zA-Z]+[a-zA-Z0-9._]+@[a-zA-Z]+\.[a-zA-Z.]{2,5}/i);
}

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) { 
        vm = this.vm;
	
        ConfigureD2MShipment("this.NewShipment");
	
        this.vm.PredefinedReturnAddress =  GetReturnAddresses();
	
		var returnTabInterval = setInterval(function(){
									
									var tabIsLoaded = $("#cboPredefinedReturnAddress select");
		
									if (tabIsLoaded)
									{
										clearInterval(returnTabInterval);
										if (IsEventAttached($("#cboPredefinedReturnAddress select"), "change", OnCboReturnAddressChange) === false)
										{				
											debugger;
											$("#cboPredefinedReturnAddress select").on("change", OnCboReturnAddressChange);																
										}                   
									}
							},50);		

// ConfigureD2MShipment(calleeMethod) // returns void
    function ConfigureD2MShipment(calleeMethod){
        
        debugger;
        		
		LogStartMethod("ConfigureD2MShipment()",calleeMethod);
					
		var infoMessage = "D2M shipment ";
		
		if (location.hash === '#!/shipping')		
		{
			if (CurrentShipperIsD2MEnabled() && CurrentUserIsD2MEnabled()) 
			{
				infoMessage += "is ENABLED for current shipper and current user";
				
				var originAddressCompany;
				
				var originAddressLoadedInterval = setInterval(function(){
					originAddressCompany = $('[name="company"]:eq(1)').val();
					if (originAddressCompany!=undefined && originAddressCompany.length)
					{
						EnableReturn();
						clearInterval(originAddressLoadedInterval);	
					}
				},50);
			}
			else
			{
				infoMessage += "is NOT ENABLED for shipper and user";
				var isLoaded;
				var removeD2M = setInterval(function(){
					isLoaded = $('#DirectToMobileShipmentID').is(":checked");
					if (isLoaded!=undefined && (isLoaded === false || isLoaded === false))
					{													
						$('#d2m_checkbox_div_id').remove();						
						DisableReturn();
						clearInterval(removeD2M);	
					}
				},50);
				
				
			}
		}
		else
		{
			infoMessage = "WARNING " + infoMessage + "called outside of shipping action";
		}
		LogMethodInfo(infoMessage);
    }

    this.PageLoaded = function(location) {   
        if (location == '/') document.location = '#!/shipping';
        
        $('body').delegate('*', 'focus', function () { $('div[role="alert"]:visible').hide(); })
        $('body').on('click', 'input[ng-click="vm.opendeliverDate()"], button[ng-click="vm.opendeliverDate()"]', translateDates);
        $('a[href="/Manage"][title="Manage"]').remove();

        
        setInterval(function() {
            translateDates();
            $('button').each(function() {
                const frenchMonths = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                let text = $(this).text().trim();
                let month = text.split(' ')[0];

                $('button.btn.btn-sm.btn-info.uib-datepicker-current.ng-binding').each(function() {
                    let text = $(this).text().trim();
                    if (text === 'Today') {
                        $(this).text('Aujourd\'hui');  // Translate "Today" to French
                    }
                });
                $('button.btn.btn-sm.btn-danger.uib-clear.ng-binding').each(function() {
                    let text = $(this).text().trim();
                    if (text === 'Clear') {
                        $(this).text('Effacer');  // Translate "Clear" to French
                    }
                });

                $('button.btn.btn-sm.btn-success.pull-right.uib-close.ng-binding').each(function() {
                    let text = $(this).text().trim();
                    if (text === 'Close') {
                        $(this).text('Fermer');  // Translate "Close" to French
                    }
                });
                
        
                for (let i = 0; i < frenchMonths.length; i++) {
                    if (month.includes(frenchMonths[i])) {
                        $(this).prop('disabled', true);  // Disable the button if it contains a month name
                        return false;  // Break out of the .each() loop
                    }
                }
            });
        }, 1500);

            createTranslationObjects: function() {
                return {
                    aTranslation: {"Previous": "Précédent","Next": "Suivant","All": "Tout"},
