            translateElements2: function(selector, translation, replacer) {
                $(selector).each(function() {
                    var text = $(this).val();
                    if (translation[text] !== undefined) {
                        replacer.call(this, text, translation[text]);
                    }
                });
            },
            translateElements: function(selector, translation, replacer) {
                $(selector).each(function() {
                    var text = $(this).text().trim();
                    if (translation[text] !== undefined) {
                        replacer.call(this, text, translation[text]);
                    }
                });
            },

            replaceText: function(oldText, newText) {
                this.innerHTML = this.innerHTML.replace(oldText, newText);
            },

            replaceValue: function(oldText, newText) {
                $(this).val(newText);
            },

            replaceLabel: function(oldText, newText) {
                $(this).attr('label', newText);
            },

            handleSpecificCases: function() {
                $('h5:contains("No commodities added")').text('Aucune marchandise ajoutée');
                $('label.control-label.no-left-padding.ng-binding').each(function() {
                    if ($(this).attr('style') === "text-align: center" && $(this).html() === "&nbsp;of&nbsp;&nbsp;1") {
                        $(this).html('&nbsp;de&nbsp;&nbsp;1');
                    }
                });
            },
        };

        var intervalId = setInterval(function() {
            client.init(); 
            clearInterval(intervalId);
        }, 1000);

        switch(location) {
            case '/shipping':
                this.vm.translations.ThinClient.CreateAShipment = "Créer un envoi";
                break;
            case '/history':
                $("h4:first").text("Historique");
                
                break;
            // Add more cases as needed
        }
     }

// this.PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined
this.PageLoaded = function (location) {
        
        if (location == '/shipping') this.Shipping();
        else if (location == '/history') this.History();
        else if (location == '/closemanifest') this.CloseManifest();
        else if (location == '/manifestdocuments') this.ManifestDocuments();
        else if (location == '/transmit') this.Transmit();
        else if (location == '/groupmanager') this.GroupManager();
        else if (location == '/managedata') this.ManageData();
    }

// this.Shipping() // returns undefined
this.Shipping = function () {
        translateSelectAddressBookOption();
        this.vm.pickupRequestButtonCaption = client.translateToFrench['Pickup Request'];
        this.vm.translations.ThinClient.CreateAShipment = client.translateToFrench['Create a Shipment'];
        this.vm.translations.ThinClient.Reset = client.translateToFrench['Reset'];
        this.vm.translations.ThinClient.Continue = client.translateToFrench['Continue'];
        this.vm.translations.Common.Clear = client.translateToFrench['Clear'];
        this.vm.translations.Common.SelectAction = client.translateToFrench['Select Action'];
        this.vm.translations.Common.Add = client.translateToFrench['Add'];
        this.vm.translations.Common.Update = client.translateToFrench['Update'];
        this.vm.translations.Common.Today = 'hello'

        function translateSelectAddressBookOption () {
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                var $selectAddressBook = $('form[name="addressForm"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.AddressBookIdToProcess"] option[label="Select address book"]');
                if ($selectAddressBook.length >= 3) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    $selectAddressBook.each(function () {
                        if (client.translateToFrench[this.text] !== undefined) {
                            $(this).attr('label', client.translateToFrench[this.text]);
                        }
                    });
                }
            });
        }
    }

// Source: GlaxoSmithKline LLC (gsk)_Glasko Smith BR_69.cs
// function ClientBusinessRules() // returns undefined
function ClientBusinessRules() {
    var userContext;

    this.PageLoaded = function(location) {
        getUserContext();
    }

    this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        shipmentRequest.Packages.forEach(function (packageItem) {
			packageItem.MiscReference6 = shipmentRequest.ConsigneeReference;
			if (packageItem.MiscReference1 == 'Yes-Use GSK Shipper' || packageItem.MiscReference1 == 'Not Sure-Use GSK Shipper') {
		        throw({message: 'You selected ' + packageItem.MiscReference1 + '. You must select No-Continue',errorCode:'-1'});
            }
        });
    };

    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
        this.vm.NotificationAddressEmail = this.AddEmailToNotification;
        var originCustomData = GetCustomData(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress);
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = GetKeyValue('Custom1', originCustomData);
    };

    this.PreSearchHistory = function(searchCriteria) {
        debugger;
        var whereClauses = searchCriteria.WhereClauses;
        whereClauses.push({ FieldName: 'UserId', FieldValue: userContext.UserId, Operator: 5 });
    }

    this.AddEmailToNotification = function(event) {
        var currentTarget = event.currentTarget;
        var ngModelName = currentTarget.attributes['ng-model'].nodeValue.split('.').pop();
        var emailAddress = GetShipmentEmailAddresses(this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults);
        var pkg = this.currentShipment.Packages[0];

        if (ngModelName.indexOf('DeliveryException') >= 0){
            SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else if (ngModelName.indexOf('Delivery') >= 0) {
            SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else {
            SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        }
    }

    function SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, checked) {
        if (checked) {
            if (pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail == undefined || pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail.trim() == '') {
                if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                    pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress.Origin;
                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            } else {
                if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                    pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Origin;
                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            }
        } else {
            var notificationAddressEmail = pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail;
            if (ngModelName == 'ShipToNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Consignee, 'g')
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Origin, 'g')
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            }

            if (notificationAddressEmail.indexOf(',') == 0) {
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.substring(1);
            }
            pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail;
        }
    }

    function SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, checked) {
        if (checked) {
            if (pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail == undefined || pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail.trim() == '') {
                if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                    pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress.Origin;
                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            } else {
                if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                    pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Origin;
                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            }
        } else {
            var notificationAddressEmail = pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail;
            if (ngModelName == 'ShipToDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Consignee, 'g')
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Origin, 'g')
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            }

            if (notificationAddressEmail.indexOf(',') == 0) {
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.substring(1);
            }
            pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail;
        }
    }

    function SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, checked) {
        if (checked) {
            if (pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail == undefined || pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail.trim() == '') {
                if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromDeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                    pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress.Origin;
                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToDeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            } else {
                if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromDeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                    pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Origin;
                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToDeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            }
        } else {
            var notificationAddressEmail = pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail;
            if (ngModelName == 'ShipToDeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Consignee, 'g')
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromDeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Origin, 'g')
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            }

            if (notificationAddressEmail.indexOf(',') == 0) {
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.substring(1);
            }
            pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail;
        }
    }

    function GetShipmentEmailAddresses(def) {
        var emailAddress = {}
        if (def.Consignee.Email != undefined && def.Consignee.Email != '') {
            emailAddress.Consignee = def.Consignee.Email;
        }
        if (def.OriginAddress != undefined && def.OriginAddress.Email != undefined && def.OriginAddress.Email != '') {
            emailAddress.Origin = def.OriginAddress.Email;
        }
        return emailAddress;
    }

    function GetCustomData(nameAddress) {
        if (nameAddress && nameAddress.CustomData) {
            return nameAddress.CustomData;
        }
        return [];
    }

    function GetKeyValue(key, arr) {
        for (var index in arr) {
            if (arr[index].Key.toLowerCase() === key.toLowerCase()) return arr[index].Value;
        }
        return '';
    }

    function getUserContext() {
        if (userContext == undefined) {
            userContext = ajaxGet('api/usercontext/GET');
        }
    }

    function ajaxGet(url) {
        var result;
        $.ajax({
            type: 'GET',
            url: url,
            async: false,
            success: function(response) {
                result = response;
            }
        });
        return result;
    }
}

    this.PageLoaded = function (shipmentRequest, userParams, location) {

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        if (callUserMethod(1) == 'supervisor') {
            this.vm.fieldOptions["MiscReference3"].IsDisabled = false;
        }
        shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference12 = userEmail;

        // general visibility
        shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].NotificationFailureAddressEmail = userEmail;
        // ship notification
        shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].ShipNotificationEmail = true;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].ShipNotificationAddressEmail = userEmail;
        // delivery notification
        shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].DeliveryNotificationEmail = true;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = userEmail;
        // delivery exeption notification
        shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].DeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail = true;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail = userEmail;
        // return delivery notification
        shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryNotificationEmail = true;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = userEmail;
    }

// Source: HARLEY DAVIDSON (HD)_HD CBR 2.3 Fix_1758.cs
// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function (location) {

        if (location == '/') {
            var w = window.location.href + "batchmanager";
            window.location.replace(w);
        }

        if (location == '/batchmanager') {
            $(document).ready(function () {
                $.globalEval('var userContext;');

                var dataObject = {};
                dataObject.Action = "GetDealerId";
                dataObject.Content = "";
                debugger;
                var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(dataObject), UserContext: client.userContext };
                clientService.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false).done(function (jsonData) {
                    debugger;
                    //console.log(jsonData.Data);
                    $('body').find('a[ng-click="vm.itemPerPageChanged(0)"]').first().trigger('click').promise().done(function (e) {
                        ProcessDealerId(jsonData.Data);
                    });
                });
            }); //end document.ready
        }

        if (location == '/batchdetail') {
            $(document).ready(function () {
                try {
                    $('body').delegate('a[ng-model="vm.itemsPerPage"][ng-click="vm.itemPerPageChanged(0)"]', 'click', function (e) {
                        var waitForTable = setInterval(function () {
                            /* The spanTotalBatchItems element text defaults to a value of 0, need to wait until it changes before we continue. */
                            if (($('#spanTotalBatchItems').length > 0) && ($('#spanTotalBatchItems').text() != "0")) {
                                var currentDate = new Date();
                                var totalBatchItems = parseInt($('#spanTotalBatchItems').text());

                                /* Once this condition is met, we can remove the rows we don't want. */
                                if ($('#tableBatchDetails tr').length >= totalBatchItems) {
                                    clearInterval(waitForTable);
                                    //console.log('table rows condition met.');
                                    /* Loop the table rows. */
                                    $('#tableBatchDetails tr:gt(0)').each(function (x, y) {
                                        var tdDate = new Date($(this).find('td:eq(1)').text());
                                        if (tdDate < currentDate) {
                                            $(this).remove();
                                        }
                                    }).promise().done(function (e) {
                                        $('#tableBatchDetails').show();
                                        var i = $('#tableBatchDetails tr').length;
                                        $('#spanTotalBatchItems').text(i);
                                    });
                                } //end if ($('#tableBatchDetails tr').length >= totalBatchItems) 

                            } //end if (($('#spanTotalBatchItems').length > 0) && ($('#spanTotalBatchItems').text() != "0")) 

                        }, 250);
                    });

                    /* Event handler for the 'View Labels' button. */
                    $('body').delegate('#buttonViewCheckedLabels', 'click', function (e) {
                        //prevent the subsequent listeners from firing
                        e.stopImmediatePropagation();
                        // console.log("Click");
                        ViewCheckedLabels();
                        //   $('#tableBatchDetails').find('input[type=checkbox]:checked').each(function () 
                        //   { 
                        //     ViewCheckedLabels();
                        //   });
                    }); //end button delegate

                    /* Trigger the click of the 'All' button.  Maybe in the future add an id to the element to make the code a bit more readable. */
                    $('a[ng-model="vm.itemsPerPage"][ng-click="vm.itemPerPageChanged(0)"]').trigger('click');


                }
                catch (err) {
                    console.error(err.message);
                }
            }); //end document.ready

    } //end PageLoaded

                        var waitForTable = setInterval(function () {
                            /* The spanTotalBatchItems element text defaults to a value of 0, need to wait until it changes before we continue. */
                            if (($('#spanTotalBatchItems').length > 0) && ($('#spanTotalBatchItems').text() != "0")) {
                                var currentDate = new Date();
                                var totalBatchItems = parseInt($('#spanTotalBatchItems').text());

                                /* Once this condition is met, we can remove the rows we don't want. */
                                if ($('#tableBatchDetails tr').length >= totalBatchItems) {
                                    clearInterval(waitForTable);
                                    //console.log('table rows condition met.');
                                    /* Loop the table rows. */
                                    $('#tableBatchDetails tr:gt(0)').each(function (x, y) {
                                        var dueDate = new Date($(this).find('td:eq(1)').text());
                                        if (dueDate < currentDate) {
                                            $(this).remove();
                                        }
                                    }).promise().done(function (e) {
                                        $('#tableBatchDetails').show();
                                        var i = $('#tableBatchDetails tr').length;
                                        $('#spanTotalBatchItems').text(i);
                                    });
                                }
                            }
                        }, 250);
                    });

                    /* Event handler for the 'View Labels' button. */
                    $('body').delegate('#buttonViewCheckedLabels', 'click', function (e) {
                        //prevent the subsequent listeners from firing
                        e.stopImmediatePropagation();
                        // console.log("Click");
                        ViewCheckedLabels();
                    }); //end button delegate

                    /* Trigger the click of the 'All' button.  Maybe in the future add an id to the element to make the code a bit more readable. */
                    $('a[ng-model="vm.itemsPerPage"][ng-click="vm.itemPerPageChanged(0)"]').trigger('click');
                    
                    if (!$('#HazAlertShipment_panel').is(':visible')) {
		                $('#HazAlertShipment_panel').modal('show');
		                $('#HazAlertShipment_panel').on('shown.bs.modal', function() {
		                	$(this).find('[autofocus]').focus();
		                });
	                }
                }
                catch (err) {
                    console.error(err.message);
                }
            }); //end document.ready
        }
        
        if (window.location.hash == '#!/history') {
        }
        
        $('select[id="reports"]').hide();
        $('ul.navbar-nav a:contains("History")').text('Claim Search');

// function PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined

// function BatchManager() // returns undefined
    this.BatchManager = function() {
        debugger;

        // set user email
        var userEmail = $("div.navbar-collapse").text();
        userEmail = userEmail.match(/([a-zA-Z0-9._-]+@[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+\.[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+)/gi).toString();
        $("#email").val(userEmail);
        $("#email").change();

        IPSUploadFile();

        function IPSUploadFile() {
            $('body').delegate('#ipsUploadFile', 'click', function () {
                alertMessage('info', "Rate Process Started, an email will be sent upon completion");
                showSpinner();
                var vm = $(this).attr('vm')
                if (ensureLoadIPS(vm)) {
                    var fileName = cbr.loadIPS.file.name.split('.')[0];
                    debugger;
                    var reader = new FileReader();
                    reader.readAsDataURL(cbr.loadIPS.file);
                    reader.onload = function () {
                        var data = {
                            'UserContext': cbr.userContext,
                            'Data' : JSON.stringify({
                                'Action': 'Rate',
                                'Shipper': cbr.loadIPS.shipper,
                                'ShipDate': cbr.loadIPS.shipDate,
                                'Email': cbr.loadIPS.email,
                                'FileName': fileName,
                                'EncodedFile': this.result.split(',')[1],
                            })
                        }

                        $.post({ 
                            url: clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl + '/UserMethod',
                            data,
                            headers: clientService.authorizationToken()
                        }).done(function (result) {
                            hideSpinner();
                            if (result.ErrorCode > 0) {
                                alertMessage('danger', response.ErrorMessage);
                            } else {
                                alertMessage('success', "Rate Completed");
                                loadIPSReset();
                            }
                        }).fail(function (err) {
                            hideSpinner();
                            alertMessage('danger',"The process is taking longer than usual to complete but will continue to run on the server until the rate file is complete");
                        });	
                    }
                }
                // hide the spinner after 15 seconds
                setTimeout(function(){
                    hideSpinner();
                }, 15000);
            });
        }

        function loadIPSReset() {
            $.each( cbr.loadIPS, function(name, value){
                $('[ng-model="vm.loadIPS.' + name + '"]').val(null);
            });
        }

        function ensureLoadIPS(vm) {
            var msg = [];
            var result = true;

            if (vm == '') {
                msg.push('Please update all options and try again.');
            } else {
                cbr.loadIPS = JSON.parse(vm);
                //if (cbr.loadIPS.type == undefined) msg.push('\u2022Select Rate or Address Validation radio button.');
                if (cbr.loadIPS.shipper == undefined) msg.push('\u2022Missing Shipper.');
                if (cbr.loadIPS.shipDate == undefined) msg.push("\u2022Missing Ship Date.");
                if (cbr.loadIPS.email == undefined) {
                    msg.push('\u2022Missing Email Address.');
                } else {
                    if (invalidEmailAddress(cbr.loadIPS.email)) msg.push('\u2022Email Address is invalid.')
                }

                var files = $('#ipsFileInputField').prop('files');
                if (files.length == 0) {
                    msg.push('\u2022Missing File.')
                } else {
                    cbr.loadIPS.file = files[0];
                }
            }

            if (msg.length > 0) {
                result = false;
                alertMessage('danger', msg.join("<br />"));
                hideSpinner();
            }
            
            return result;
        }
    }

    this.ManifestDocuments = function () {

        function testbutton() {
            $('body').delegate('#buttonExportCODFile', 'click', function () {
                debugger;
                var shipper = $(this).attr('shipper');
                var carrier = $(this).attr('carrier');
                var historyId = $(this).attr('historyId');
                var historyShipDateYear = $(this).attr('shipDateYear');
                var historyShipDateMonth = $(this).attr('shipDateMonth');
                var historyShipDateDay = $(this).attr('shipDateDay');
                var isSftpChecked = $('#SftprBtnId').prop('checked');
                var isLocalChecked = $('#LocalrBtnId').prop('checked');
                debugger;

                // Send data to user method on the server side
                var usermethodParams = { "action": 1, "usercontext": client.userContext, "shipper": shipper, "historyId": historyId, "historyShipDateYear": historyShipDateYear, "historyShipDateMonth": historyShipDateMonth, "historyShipDateDay": historyShipDateDay, "carrier": carrier, "sftpSelectrdStatus": isSftpChecked, "localSelectrdStatus": isLocalChecked };
                var codFileString;

                var data = { UserContext: client.userContext, "Data": JSON.stringify(usermethodParams) };
                
                clientService.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false).done(function (response) {
                    debugger;                  

                    //****New code 01.24.2022****
                    var jsonString = $("<textarea/>").html(response.Data).text();

                    if (jsonString && isLocalChecked) {                        
                        codFileString = jsonString;

                        var data = new Blob([codFileString], { type: 'text/plain' });

                        var ie = navigator.userAgent.match(/MSIE\s([\d.]+)/),
                            ie11 = navigator.userAgent.match(/Trident\/7.0/) && navigator.userAgent.match(/rv:11/),
                            ieEdge = navigator.userAgent.match(/Edge/g),
                            ieVer = (ie ? ie[1] : (ie11 ? 11 : (ieEdge ? 12 : -1)));

                        // set the export file name 
                        var exportFileName = "ShipmentRequest" + historyShipDateYear + historyShipDateMonth + historyShipDateDay + "_1_" + shipper + ".txt"

                        if (ieVer > -1) {
                            window.navigator.msSaveBlob(codFileString, exportFileName);

                        } else {
                            var downloadLink = document.createElement("a");
                            downloadLink.download = exportFileName;
                            downloadLink.href = window.URL.createObjectURL(data);
                            downloadLink.style.display = "none";
                            document.body.appendChild(downloadLink);
                            downloadLink.click();
                            document.body.removeChild(link);
                        }
                    }
                });          
            })
        }
    }

// Source: KeithCo (KC)_Address Validation CBR (sna6dxb)_2447.cs
// function ClientBusinessRules() // returns undefined
function ClientBusinessRules()
{
  this.PageLoaded = function (location)
  {
    if (location == '/shipping')
    {
      $('div.row.top-tool-bar:first').find('.pull-left:first').append($('<button>').attr('id', 'btnValidateAddress').addClass('btn btn-xs btn-primary').text('Validate Address'));

      $('#btnValidateAddress').on('click', (e) =>
      {
        console.log('GetNewGuid()', TOOLS.GetNewGuid());
        console.log('GetRandomNumber(13)', TOOLS.GetRandomNumber(13));
        console.log('GetRandomAlphaString(21)', TOOLS.GetRandomAlphaString(21));
        console.log('GetRandomAlphaNumericString(32)', TOOLS.GetRandomAlphaNumericString(32));
        console.log('GetRandomStringWithSpecialCharacters(48)', TOOLS.GetRandomStringWithSpecialCharacters(48));

        TOOLS.WaitForElement('[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]:first', 'FOCUSED', true).then((result) => console.log(result));

        AJAX.MakeAsyncUserMethodRequest({ "MethodName": "ValidateAddress", "MethodData": JSON.stringify(VALIDATE.Address()) }).then((result) =>
        {
          result.length === 1 ? $('#btnValidateAddress').addClass('btn-success') : null;
        });
      });
    }
  }

  this.NewShipment = (shipmentRequest) => {}

  const VALIDATE = (() =>
  {
    return {

      Address: () =>
      {
        const eConsigneeInputs = $('[nameaddress="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee"]').find('input, select');
        let addressObject = {};

        $(eConsigneeInputs).each((k, input) =>
        {
          const [keyName, keyValue] = [$(input).attr('name'), $(input).val().replace('string:', '')];

          if (keyName && keyValue)
          {
            const properCaseKeyName = keyName.slice(0, 1).toUpperCase() + keyName.slice(1);
            addressObject[properCaseKeyName] = keyValue;
          }
        });

        return addressObject;
      }
    }
  })();

  const TOOLS = (() =>
  {
    /**
    @param {number} iCharLength - Number of characters to return.
    @param {string} charType - Either 'integer', 'string', or 'mixed' (alphanumeric).
    @return {string} Random characters.
    @author Don Beal <dbeal@ups.com>
    **/
    const getRandomCharacters = (iCharLength, charType) =>
    {
      let charList = '';
      switch (charType)
      {
        case 'integer':
          charList = '123456789';
          break;
        case 'string':
          charList = 'ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz';
          break;
        case 'mixed':
          charList = 'ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789';
          break;
        case 'all':
          charList = 'ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789!@#$%^&*()[]{}~<>.?';
      }

      return ([...Array(iCharLength)].map(() => charList.charAt(Math.floor(Math.random() * charList.length))).join(''));
    }

    /**
    @param {object} jsonObject - Object to traverse to remove trailing spaces from keys and values.
    @return {object} Trimmed source jsonObject.
    @author Don Beal <dbeal@ups.com>
    **/
    const trimAllKeysAndValues = (jsonObject) =>
    {
      for (const key in jsonObject)
      {
        if (typeof jsonObject[key] == "object" && jsonObject[key] !== null)
        {
          trimAllKeysAndValues(jsonObject[key]);
        }
        else if (jsonObject.hasOwnProperty(key))
        {
          jsonObject[key] = (typeof jsonObject[key] == 'string' ? jsonObject[key].trim() : jsonObject[key]);
        }
      }

      return jsonObject;
    }

    return {

      /**
      @param {any} anyOne - First object or string to compare.
      @param {any} anyTwo - Second object or string to compare.
      @param {boolean} bTakeOne - If strings don't match, return the anyOne variable.
      @param {boolean} bTakeTwo - If strings don't match, return the anyTwo variable.
      @return {any} Boolean if strings match and bTakeOne or bTakeTwo is null.
      @author Don Beal <dbeal@ups.com>
      **/
      CompareObjectsAndStrings: (anyOne, anyTwo, bTakeOne, bTakeTwo) =>
      {

        let [stringOne, stringTwo] = [anyOne, anyTwo];

        if (typeof anyOne == "object")
        {
          stringOne = trimAllKeysAndValues(anyOne);
          stringTwo = trimAllKeysAndValues(anyTwo);
        }

        const bMatch = JSON.stringify(stringOne).toUpperCase() == JSON.stringify(stringTwo).toUpperCase();

        return bMatch && bTakeOne ? anyOne : bMatch && bTakeTwo ? anyTwo : bMatch;
      },

      /**
       @return {string}
       @author Don Beal <dbeal@ups.com>
      **/
      GetNewGuid: () =>
      {
        return URL.createObjectURL(new Blob([])).slice(-36);
      },

      /**
      @param {number} iCharLength - Number of characters to return.
      @return {string}
      @author Don Beal <dbeal@ups.com>
      **/
      GetRandomAlphaString: (iCharLength) =>
      {
        return getRandomCharacters(iCharLength, 'string');
      },

      /**
      @param {number} iCharLength - Number of characters to return.
      @return {string}
      @author Don Beal <dbeal@ups.com>
      **/
      GetRandomAlphaNumericString: (iCharLength) =>
      {
        return getRandomCharacters(iCharLength, 'mixed');
      },

      /**
      @param {number} iCharLength - Number of characters to return.
      @return {string} Returns string as returning large numbers will return odd values.
      @author Don Beal <dbeal@ups.com>
      **/
      GetRandomNumber: (iCharLength) =>
      {
        return getRandomCharacters(iCharLength, 'integer');
      },

      /**
      @param {number} iCharLength - Number of characters to return.
      @return {string}
      @author Don Beal <dbeal@ups.com>
      **/
      GetRandomStringWithSpecialCharacters: (iCharLength) =>
      {
        return getRandomCharacters(iCharLength, 'all');
      },

      /**
      @desc Wait for an element to enter the DOM so it can be manipulated.
      @param {string} eElement - Element selector like '[name=Consignee]' or '#divMain'.
      @param {string} inputValue - Default value for input elements (optional).
      @param {boolean} bFocus - Focus on the passed element once it is found (optional).
      @return {boolean} TRUE for resolve, FALSE for reject.
      @author Don Beal <dbeal@ups.com>
      **/
      WaitForElement: async (eElement, inputValue, bFocus) =>
      {
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) =>
        {
          let i = 0;
          const timer = window.setInterval(() =>
          {
            if ($(eElement).length > 0)
            {
              inputValue ? $(eElement).val(inputValue) : undefined;
              bFocus ? $(eElement).focus().select() : undefined;

              resolve(true);
              window.clearInterval(timer);
            }

            if (i === 9)
            {
              reject(false);
              window.clearInterval(timer);
            }

            i++
          }, 200);
        })
      }
    }
  })();

  const AJAX = (() =>
  {
    let authToken;
    let userContext;
    let urlUserContext;
    let urlShipExecService;

    return {

      SetRequestVariables: () =>
      {
        return $.getJSON({ url: 'config.json' }).done((config) =>
        {
          urlUserContext = config.ShipExecServiceUrl.replace('ShippingService', 'usercontext/GET');
          urlShipExecService = config.ShipExecServiceUrl;

          if (window.localStorage.getItem('TCToken'))
            authToken = { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + JSON.parse(window.localStorage.getItem("TCToken")).access_token };

          return config;
        });
      },

      MakeAsyncUserMethodRequest: (RequestObject) =>
      {
        let defer = new $.Deferred();

        AJAX.SetRequestVariables().done(() =>
        {
          $.get({ url: urlUserContext, headers: authToken }).done((e) => e).then((context) =>
          {
            userContext = context;

            let m = {};
            m.UserContext = userContext;
            m.Data = JSON.stringify(RequestObject);

            $.post({ url: urlShipExecService + '/UserMethod', data: m, headers: authToken }).done((result) =>
            {
              console.log(result.Data);
              defer.resolve(JSON.parse(atob(result.Data)));
            });
          });
        });

        return defer.promise();
      }

    }
  })();
}

// this.PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
  this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest)
  {
    //debugger;
    loadValue = loadValue.replace('!!', '');

    if (typeof shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 !== 'undefined' && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5.length > 2)
    {
      alertMessage('danger', shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5);
    }

    this.vm.getWeight();
    //$("#overrideRateShopping_Y").prop("checked", true);

    // Warn user if expedited service selected and PO box is checked
    const expServices = "UPS.NDA,UPS.2AM,UPS.2DA,UPS.EXP,USPS.PRIORITY,USPS.EXPR".split(',');

    let hasExpedited = expServices.some(service => shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol.includes(service));
    if (hasExpedited && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.PoBox)
    {
      alertMessage('warning', "Order " + loadValue + " has an Expedited service selected but a PO box was used. Contact Customer Service for a new address.")
    }

    // if Int'l shipment, show Assign Commodities button, hide Add Package button group, and init AssignGoods
    //sna6dxb - 09-23-2022
    //don't need this any longer, the button is hidden by default in the template
    //$('#btnAssignCommodities').hide();
    if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country !== "US")
    {
      $('#btnAssignCommodities').show();
      $('button[title="Add Package"]').parent().hide();
      const Goods = new AssignGoods(this.vm);
    }
    else {
        // ensure Assign Commodities button is hidden in case they load an Int'l order by mistake, then load domestic
        $('#btnAssignCommodities').hide();
        $('button[title="Add Package"]').parent().show();
    }
  }

// this.GetViewModelFromTemplate(viewModel) // returns void
  this.GetViewModelFromTemplate = function(viewModel)
  {
    vm = viewModel;
  }

   function GetKeyValue(key, arr) {
      for (var index in arr) {
          if (arr[index].Key.toLowerCase() === key.toLowerCase()) return arr[index].Value;
      }
      return '';
  }
function ConvertStateAbbr(input) {
    var states = [
        ['Alabama', 'AL'],
        ['Alaska', 'AK'],
        ['American Samoa', 'AS'],
        ['Arizona', 'AZ'],
        ['Arkansas', 'AR'],
        ['Armed Forces Americas', 'AA'],
        ['Armed Forces Europe', 'AE'],
        ['Armed Forces Pacific', 'AP'],
        ['California', 'CA'],
        ['Colorado', 'CO'],
        ['Connecticut', 'CT'],
        ['Delaware', 'DE'],
        ['District Of Columbia', 'DC'],
        ['Florida', 'FL'],
        ['Georgia', 'GA'],
        ['Guam', 'GU'],
        ['Hawaii', 'HI'],
        ['Idaho', 'ID'],
        ['Illinois', 'IL'],
        ['Indiana', 'IN'],
        ['Iowa', 'IA'],
        ['Kansas', 'KS'],
        ['Kentucky', 'KY'],
        ['Louisiana', 'LA'],
        ['Maine', 'ME'],
        ['Marshall Islands', 'MH'],
        ['Maryland', 'MD'],
        ['Massachusetts', 'MA'],
        ['Michigan', 'MI'],
        ['Minnesota', 'MN'],
        ['Mississippi', 'MS'],
        ['Missouri', 'MO'],
        ['Montana', 'MT'],
        ['Nebraska', 'NE'],
        ['Nevada', 'NV'],
        ['New Hampshire', 'NH'],
        ['New Jersey', 'NJ'],
        ['New Mexico', 'NM'],
        ['New York', 'NY'],
        ['North Carolina', 'NC'],
        ['North Dakota', 'ND'],
        ['Northern Mariana Islands', 'NP'],
        ['Ohio', 'OH'],
        ['Oklahoma', 'OK'],
        ['Oregon', 'OR'],
        ['Pennsylvania', 'PA'],
        ['Puerto Rico', 'PR'],
        ['Rhode Island', 'RI'],
        ['South Carolina', 'SC'],
        ['South Dakota', 'SD'],
        ['Tennessee', 'TN'],
        ['Texas', 'TX'],
        ['US Virgin Islands', 'VI'],
        ['Utah', 'UT'],
        ['Vermont', 'VT'],
        ['Virginia', 'VA'],
        ['Washington', 'WA'],
        ['West Virginia', 'WV'],
        ['Wisconsin', 'WI'],
        ['Wyoming', 'WY'],
    ];

    input = input.replace(/\w\S*/g, function (txt) { return txt.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + txt.substr(1).toLowerCase(); });
    for (var state of states) {
        if (state[0] == input) {
            return (state[1]);
        }
    }

}

function GetUserContext() {
    if (userContext === undefined) {
        userContext = ajaxGet('api/usercontext/GET');
    }
}
function ajaxGet(url) {
    var result;
    $.ajax({
        type: "GET",
        url: url,
        async: false,
        success: function(response) {
            result = response;
        }
    });
    return result;
}
// End ClientBusinessRules
}

// this.PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined
    this.PageLoaded = function (location) {

// this.Shipping() // returns undefined
    this.Shipping = function () {
        $(document).ready(function () {
            client.setDivReference3();

        })

        $('body').delegate('select[name="ConsigneeReference_txt"]', 'change', this.vm, consigneeReferenceOnChange);

        function consigneeReferenceOnChange(e) {

            client.vm = e.data;
            if (e.target.value == 'string:Ambient')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(3, true);
            else if (e.target.value == 'string:Refrigerated')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(5, true);
            else if (e.target.value == 'string:Ambient/Refrigerated Combo Box')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(6, true);
            else if (e.target.value == 'string:Frozen')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(6, false, true);
            else if (e.target.value == 'string:Frozen/Ambient Combo Box')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(6, false, true);

        }

        function changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(weightAmount, isHidden, isRequired) {
            $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]').val(weightAmount).change();
            if (isHidden) client.$divReference3.hide();
            else client.$divReference3.show();
            client.$divReference3.find('input').css('border-color', isRequired ? '#a94442' : client.defaultMiscReference3BorderColor);
            client.vm.fieldOptions.MiscReference3.IsRequired = isRequired;
        }

    }

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {


        clearUploadMessages();
        this.clearSessionState();
        setUploadDelegates(shipmentRequest);
        this.currentShipment = shipmentRequest;


        if (location == '/shipping') {
            StudyReferenceCodeModal.InitElements(false);
            $('#LoadStudyReferenceCodeData').click();
            Tools.HideLoader();
        }

        client?.$divReference3?.hide();

        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address;

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[0].Value; //Study Reference code

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[1].Value;  //Protocol Number

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[2].Value;  //Site Number

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4 = true;

        //Storing StudyReference codes on the Miscreference17
        var studyReferenceCode = null;
        var studyReferenceCodeList = [];
        for (var i = 0; i < this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference17.FieldOptionValidations.length; i++) {
            debugger;
            studyReferenceCode = this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference17.FieldOptionValidations[i].Value.split(',').map(x => x.trim());
            studyReferenceCodeList.push(studyReferenceCode);
        }
        var shipper = null;
        $(document).ready(function () {

            $("#OK").on("click", function () {
                debugger;
                var selectedValue = $('#selectShipper').val().trim();
                var shipperReferenceVal = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();
                var arrayOrders = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(shipperReferenceVal);
                if (arrayOrders.includes(selectedValue)) {
                    var selectedIndex = arrayOrders.indexOf(selectedValue);
                    var selectedStudy = arrayOrders[selectedIndex];
                    //Populating the entered Study Reference code in the Shipper reference field.
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val(selectedStudy);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();

                    var miscReference1Val = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val();
                    var arrayOrders1 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(miscReference1Val);
                    var selectedProtocol = arrayOrders1[selectedIndex];
                    //Populating the corresponding Protocol number in the Misc reference 1 field.
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val(selectedProtocol);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val();

                    debugger;
                    var miscReference2Val = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val();
                    var arrayOrders2 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(miscReference2Val);
                    var selectedSite = arrayOrders2[selectedIndex];
                    //Populating the corresponding Site number in the Misc reference 2 field.
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val(selectedSite);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val();

                    //Assigning Shipper based on StudyReferenceCode available on validation list
                    for (var j = 0; j < studyReferenceCodeList.length; j++) {
                        var firstCode = studyReferenceCodeList[j];
                        if (firstCode.length >= 2 && firstCode[0] == selectedValue) {
                            shipper = "string:" + firstCode[1];
                            $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"]').val(shipper);
                            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"] option:selected').val().split(":")[1];


                        }
                    }

                }
                else {
                    alert("Please contact Marken to have this study added to your profile.");
                    throw new Error("Please contact Marken to have this study added to your profile.");
                }

                //Calling the SBR Usermethod to get the Shipper Friendly name.    
                //GetUserShipper(selectedStudy, shipmentRequest);

                StudyReferenceCodeModal.CloseDialogWithoutSaving();

            });

        });

        //Setting Proactive recovery
        $(document).ready(function () {
            debugger;
            $('body').delegate('[property="ProactiveRecovery"]', 'change', function (e) {
                debugger;
                if (e.target.checked == true) {
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecovery = true;
                    $('select option[value="number:1"]').prop("selected", true);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecoveryType = 1;
                    var total = 0;
                    for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions.length; i++) {
                        total += shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions[i]
                    }
                    var inst = [];
                    inst.push(total);
                    debugger;
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecoveryInstructions = inst[0].toString();

                }
                else {
                    $('select option[selected="selected"]').prop("selected", true);
                }
            });


        });

    }

this.PageLoaded = function (location) {

                //Hiding the PDF Upload

                $('#btnUploadPdfGoodsClear').hide();
                $('#uploadSuccessLabel').hide();

                $('body').delegate('[ng-click="vm.addCommodity()"]', 'click', function () {
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        $('[heading="Export Quantity"]').hide();
                        $('[heading="License"]').hide();
                        $('[heading="Origin Manufacture Address"]').hide();
                        $('[heading="NAFTA"]').hide();
                        $('[heading="Restricted Article"]').hide();
                        $('[heading="Document Methods"]').hide();
                        $('[heading="DDTC"]').hide();
                        $('[property="CommodityContent.CommodityCondition"]').hide();
                        $('[name="originDescription_txt"]').hide();
                    }, 150);

                });
            });
            
        }
    }

// Shipping() // returns undefined
this.Shipping = function () {
        $(document).ready(function () {
            client.setDivReference3();

        })

        $('body').delegate('select[name="ConsigneeReference_txt"]', 'change', this.vm, consigneeReferenceOnChange);

        function consigneeReferenceOnChange(e) {

            client.vm = e.data;
            if (e.target.value == 'string:Ambient')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(1, true);
            else if (e.target.value == 'string:Refrigerated')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(5, true);

        }

        function changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(weightAmount, isHidden, isRequired) {
            $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]').val(weightAmount).change();
            if (isHidden) client.$divReference3.hide();
            else client.$divReference3.show();
            client.$divReference3.find('input').css('border-color', isRequired ? '#a94442' : client.defaultMiscReference3BorderColor);
            client.vm.fieldOptions.MiscReference3.IsRequired = isRequired;
        }

    }

this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {

        debugger;
        clearUploadMessages();
        this.clearSessionState();
        setUploadDelegates(shipmentRequest);
        this.currentShipment = shipmentRequest;
            
        client?.$divReference3?.hide();
        
        //Setting Proactive recovery
        $(document).ready(function () {
            debugger;
            $('body').delegate('[property="ProactiveRecovery"]', 'change', function (e) {
                debugger;
                if (e.target.checked == true) {
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecovery = true;
                    $('select option[value="number:1"]').prop("selected", true);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecoveryType = 1;
                    var total = 0;
                    for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions.length; i++) {
                        total += shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions[i]
                    }
                    var inst = [];
                    inst.push(total);
                    debugger;
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecoveryInstructions = inst[0].toString();

                }
                else {
                    $('select option[selected="selected"]').prop("selected", true);
                }
            });


        });

        //Adding commodities automatically.
        this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].CommodityContents = [];
                            
                            var newCommodity = {
                                Description: "UN3373 Biological Substance,Cat B",
                                Quantity: 1,
                                QuantityUnitMeasure: "EA",
                                UnitWeight:
                                    {
                                        Amount: 0.5,       
                                        Units: "KG"         
                                      },
                                UnitValue:{
                                    Amount:5,
                                    Currency:"GBP"
                                } , 
                                OriginCountry: "GB",
                                RestrictedArticleType:32,
                                HarmonizedCode:"3002901000",
                                ProductCode:"UN3733"
                            };
                                this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].CommodityContents.push(newCommodity);
                                setTimeout(function(){
                                                $('[value="Save"]').trigger('click');
                                },200);

    }

// Shipping() // returns void
    this.Shipping = function () {
        $(document).ready(function () {
            client.setDivReference3();

        })

        $('body').delegate('select[name="ConsigneeReference_txt"]', 'change', this.vm, consigneeReferenceOnChange);

        function consigneeReferenceOnChange(e) {

            client.vm = e.data;
            if (e.target.value == 'string:Ambient')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(3, true);
            else if (e.target.value == 'string:Refrigerated')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(5, true);
            else if (e.target.value == 'string:Ambient/Refrigerated Combo Box')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(6, true);
            else if (e.target.value == 'string:Frozen')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(6, false, true);
            else if (e.target.value == 'string:Frozen/Ambient Combo Box')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(6, false, true);

        }

        function changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(weightAmount, isHidden, isRequired) {
            $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]').val(weightAmount).change();
            if (isHidden) {
                client.$divReference3.hide();
                client.$divReference3.find('input').val('');
                client.vm.currentShipment.Packages[client.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference3='';
            }
            else {
                client.$divReference3.show();
            }
            client.$divReference3.find('input').css('border-color', isRequired ? '#a94442' : client.defaultMiscReference3BorderColor);
            client.vm.fieldOptions.MiscReference3.IsRequired = isRequired;
        }

    }

                Tools.ShowOverlay();

                $('#selectShipper').empty();

                $('#divModalLoadShipments').fadeIn('fast').promise().done(function () {

                });
            }

// function ClientBusinessRules() // returns void
function ClientBusinessRules() {

    var that = this;

    this.currentShipment = {};


    this.Keystroke = function (shipmentRequest, event) { }

    this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        //debugger;
        if (this.vm.profile.Name == "Outbound Labels Leg 2 Allowed User Profile") {
            //Setting Leg2 Company
            if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 == null || shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 == '') {
                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[3].Value;
            }

            //Setting Leg2 Shipper
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[2].Value;
        }

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference16 = sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataGoods');
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference17 = sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataModal');
    }

    this.clearSessionState = function () {
        sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataGoods', '');
        sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataModal', '');
        sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataGoodsFileName', '');
        sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataModalFileName', '');
    }

    this.PostShip = function (shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) {
        //debugger;
        $('#Leg2LabelRequired').prop('checked', false);
        $('#DryIceRequired').prop('checked', false);
        $('#CentralLabsFrozenSamplesReturn').prop('checked', false);
        $('#Leg2PackageWeight').val('');
        $('#Leg2DryIceWeight').val('');
        $('#Leg2DryIceWeight').hide();
        $('#quantity').val('');
        $('#EmptyPackaging').prop('checked', false);
        $('#displayMessage').hide();

        // Clear the upload error modal text
        $('#uploadErrorModalLabel').html('');

        var userData1 = shipmentResponse.Packages[0].UserData1;
        var userData2 = shipmentResponse.Packages[0].UserData2;

        if (userData1) {
            var result = JSON.parse(userData1.replace(/'/g, '"'));
            //debugger;
            this.setResponseLabel('uploadSuccessLabel', result);
        }

        if (userData2) {
            var result = JSON.parse(userData2.replace(/'/g, '"'));
            //debugger;
            this.setResponseLabel('uploadSuccessLabel', result);
        }

    }

    this.setResponseLabel = function (responseLabelId, result, sessionStorageErrorFileName) {
        console.log("Upload Response: " + result);

        var label = $('#' + responseLabelId);
        if (label) {

            //debugger;

            if (sessionStorageErrorFileName) {
                var errorMessage = "Upload failed for document "
                    + sessionStorageErrorFileName
                    + " - document exceeds maximum size (1.0 MB)";

                $('#uploadErrorModalLabel').html(errorMessage);
                $('#uploadErrorModal').modal('show');
            }

            else if (!result.Success) {
                // If the call is not successful, display an error message in a modal
                //debugger;
                var existingMessage = $('#uploadErrorModalLabel').html();

                // Creates the error message
                var errorMessage = "Upload failed for document "
                    + result.FileName
                    + " during Leg "
                    + result.Leg
                    + ".";

                // If there is an existing error message, append to it
                if (existingMessage && existingMessage.length > 0) {
                    errorMessage = existingMessage + '<br /><br />' + errorMessage;
                }

                $('#uploadErrorModalLabel').html(errorMessage);
                $('#uploadErrorModal').modal('show');
            }
        }
    }

    var clientService = {
        config: $.getJSON({
            url: 'config.json',
            async: false
        }).responseJSON,
        authorizationToken: function () {
            if (JSON.parse(window.localStorage.getItem("TCToken")))
                return {
                    'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + JSON.parse(window.localStorage.getItem("TCToken")).access_token
                };
        }
    }

    var client = {
        userContext: function () {
            var userContextUrl = 'api/usercontext/GET';
            var shipExecServiceUrl = clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
            if (shipExecServiceUrl.startsWith('http')) {
                var url = new URL(shipExecServiceUrl);
                userContextUrl = url.origin + '/' + userContextUrl;
            }
            var authorizationToken = clientService.authorizationToken();
            return $.get({
                url: userContextUrl,
                headers: authorizationToken,
                async: false
            }).responseJSON;
        }(),

    }

    //ClientService1 for Manual Upload
    var clientService1 = {
        config: $.getJSON({ url: 'config.json', async: false }).responseJSON,
        getAuthorizationToken: function () {
            if (JSON.parse(window.localStorage.getItem("TCToken")))
                return { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + JSON.parse(window.localStorage.getItem("TCToken")).access_token };
            return '';
        },
        getUserContext: function () {
            var userContextUrl = clientService1.config.ShipExecServiceUrl.replace('ShippingService', 'usercontext/GET');
            var authorizationToken = clientService1.getAuthorizationToken();
            return $.get({ url: userContextUrl, headers: authorizationToken, async: false }).responseJSON;;
        },

        thinclientService1APIRequest: function (method, data, isAsync) {

            var shipExecServiceUrl = clientService1.config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
            var authorizationToken = clientService1.getAuthorizationToken();
            return $.post({ url: shipExecServiceUrl + '/' + method, data: data, async: isAsync, headers: authorizationToken });

        }

    }
    clientService1.userContext = clientService1.getUserContext();

    //Fetching the commodity contents imported on management studio
    function GetCommodityContents() {
        var jsonData;
        var data = { "CompanyId": "0212c890-3ae4-4690-82a4-0c4ef8cd49c6", "SearchCriteria": {} };
        var ajaxRequest = clientService1.thinclientService1APIRequest('GetCommodityContents', data, false);
        jsonData = ajaxRequest.responseJSON;
        return jsonData;
    }
